          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.57"> madhurāmlarasaṃ rūkṣaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ laghu |57| nāryāstu
            madhuraṃ stanyaṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ himam ||57|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.58"> nasyāścyotanayoḥ pathyaṃ jīvanaṃ laghu dīpanam |58|
            hastinyā madhuraṃ vṛṣyaṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ guru ||58|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.59">snigdhaṃ sthairyakaraṃ śītaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ balavardhanam |59|
            prāyaḥ prābhātikaṃ kṣīraṃ guru viṣṭambhi śītalam ||59|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.60"> rātryāḥ somaguṇatvāc ca vyāyāmābhāvatas tathā |60|
            divākarābhitaptānāṃ vyāyāmānilasevanāt ||60|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.61"> śramaghnaṃ vātanuccaiva cakṣuṣyaṃ cāparāhṇikam |61|
            payo 'bhiṣyandi gurvāmaṃ prāyaśaḥ parikīrtitam ||61|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.62"> tadevoktaṃ laghutaramanabhiṣyandi vai śṛtam |62|
            varjayitvā striyāḥ stanyamāmam eva hi taddhitam ||62|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.63"> dhāroṣṇaṃ guṇavat kṣīraṃ viparītamato 'nyathā |63|
            tadevātiśṛtaṃ śītaṃ guru bṛṃhaṇamucyate ||63|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.64"> aniṣṭagandhamamlaṃ ca vivarṇaṃ virasaṃ ca yat | varjyaṃ
            salavaṇaṃ kṣīraṃ yac ca vigrathitaṃ bhavet ||64|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.65"> iti kṣīravargaḥ | atha dadhivargaḥ | dadhi tu
            madhuramamlamatyamlaṃ ceti; tatkaṣāyānurasaṃ snigdhamuṣṇaṃ
            pīnasaviṣamajvarātisārārocakamūtrakṛcchrakārśyāpahaṃ vṛṣyaṃ prāṇakaraṃ
            maṅgalyaṃ ca ||65|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.66"> mahābhiṣyandi madhuraṃ kaphamedovivardhanam |
            kaphapittakṛdamlaṃ syādatyamlaṃ raktadūṣaṇam ||66|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.67"> vidāhi sṛṣṭaviṇmūtraṃ mandajātaṃ tridoṣakṛt |67|
            snigdhaṃ vipāke madhuraṃ dīpanaṃ balavardhanam ||67|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.68"> vātāpahaṃ pavitraṃ ca dadhi gavyaṃ rucipradam |68|
            dadhyājaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ laghu vātakṣayāpaham ||68|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.69"> durnāmaśvāsakāseṣu hitamagneś ca dīpanam |69| vipāke
            madhuraṃ vṛṣyaṃ vātapittaprasādanam ||69|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.70">balāsavardhanaṃ snigdhaṃ viśeṣāddadhi māhiṣam |70| vipāke
            kaṭu sakṣāraṃ guru bhedyauṣṭrikaṃ dadhi ||70|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.71">vātamarśāṃsi kuṣṭhāni kṛmīn hantyudarāṇi ca |71| kopanaṃ
            kaphavātānāṃ durnāmnāṃ cāvikaṃ dadhi ||71|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.72"> rase pāke ca madhuramatyabhiṣyandi doṣalam |72|
            dīpanīyamacakṣuṣyaṃ vāḍavaṃ dadhi vātalam ||72|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.73"> rūkṣamuṣṇaṃ kaṣāyaṃ ca kaphamūtrāpahaṃ ca tat |73|
            snigdhaṃ vipāke madhuraṃ balyaṃ santarpaṇaṃ guru ||73|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.74"> cakṣuṣyamagryaṃ doṣaghnaṃ dadhi nāryā guṇottaram |74|
            laghu pāke balāsaghnaṃ vīryoṣṇaṃ paktināśanam ||74|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.75.1">kaṣāyānurasaṃ nāgyā dadhi varcovivardhanam |75| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.75.2">dadhīnyuktāni yānīha gavyādīni pṛthak pṛthak ||75|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.76"> vijñeyamevaṃ sarveṣu gavyam eva guṇottaram |76| vātaghnaṃ
            kaphakṛt snigdhaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ nātipittakṛt ||76|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.77"> kuryād bhaktābhilāṣaṃ ca dadhi yat suparisrutam |77| śṛtāt
            kṣīrāt tu yajjātaṃ guṇavaddadhi tat smṛtam ||77|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.78">vātapittaharaṃ rucyaṃ dhātvagnibalavardhanam |78| dadhnaḥ
            saro gururvṛṣyo vijñeyo 'nilanāśanaḥ ||78|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.79"> vahnervidhamanaś cāpi kaphaśukravivardhanaḥ |79| dadhi
            tvasāraṃ rūkṣaṃ ca grāhi viṣṭambhi vātalam ||79|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.80"> dīpanīyaṃ laghutaraṃ sakaṣāyaṃ rucipradam |80|
            śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu prāyaśo dadhi garhitam ||80|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.81.1"> hemante śiśire caiva varṣāsu dadhi śasyate |81| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.81.2"> tṛṣṇāklamaharaṃ mas tu laghu srotoviśodhanam ||81|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.82">amlaṃ kaṣāyaṃ madhuramavṛṣyaṃ kaphavātanut | prahlādanaṃ
            prīṇanaṃ ca bhinattyāśu malaṃ ca tat | balamāvahate kṣipraṃ bhaktacchandaṃ
            karoti ca ||82||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.83"> svādvamlamatyamlakamandajātaṃ tathā śṛtakṣīrabhavaṃ
            saraś ca | asāramevaṃ dadhi saptadhā'smin varge smṛtā mastuguṇās tathaiva
            ||83||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.84"> iti dadhivargaḥ | atha takravargaḥ | takraṃ tu
            madhuramamlaṃ kaṣāyānurasamuṣṇavīryaṃ laghurūkṣamagnidīpanaṃ
            garaśophātisāragrahaṇīpāṇḍurogārśaḥplīhagulmārocakaviṣamajvaratṛṣṇācchardiprasekaśūlabhedaḥśleṣmānilaharaṃ
            madhuravipākaṃ hṛdyaṃ mūtrakṛcchrasnehavyāpatpraśamanamavṛṣyaṃ ca ||84|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.85"> manthanādipṛthagbhūtasnehamardhodakaṃ ca yat |
            nātisāndradravaṃ takraṃ svādvamlaṃ tuvaraṃ rase | yat tu sasnehamajalaṃ
            mathitaṃ gholamucyate ||85|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.86"> naiva takraṃ kṣate dadyānnoṣṇakāle na durbale | na
            mūrcchābhramadāheṣu na roge raktapaittike ||86|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.87"> śītakāle 'gnimāndye ca kaphottheṣvāmayeṣu ca |
            mārgāvarodhe duṣṭe ca vāyau takraṃ praśasyate ||87|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.88"> tat punarmadhuraṃ śleṣmaprakopaṇaṃ pittapraśamanaṃ ca;
            amlaṃ vātaghnaṃ pittakaraṃ ca ||88|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.89"> vāte 'mlaṃ saindhavopetaṃ, svādu pitte saśarkaram |
            pibettakraṃ kaphe cāpi vyoṣakṣārasamanvitam ||89|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.90"> grāhiṇī vātalā rūkṣā durjarā takrakūrcikā |90|
            takrāllaghutaro maṇḍaḥ kūrcikādadhitakrajaḥ ||90|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.91"> guruḥ kilāṭo 'nilahā puṃstvanidrāpradaḥ smṛtaḥ |91|
            madhurau bṛṃhaṇau vṛṣyau tadvatpīyūṣamoraṭau ||91|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.92"> navanītaṃ punaḥ sadyaskaṃ laghu sukumāraṃ madhuraṃ
            kaṣāyamīṣadamlaṃ śītalaṃ medhyaṃ dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ saṅgrāhi pittānilaharaṃ
            vṛṣyamavidāhi kṣayakāsavraṇaśoṣārśo 'rditāpahaṃ, cirotthitaṃ guru
            kaphamedovivardhanaṃ balakaraṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ śoṣaghnaṃ viśeṣeṇa bālānāṃ
            praśasyate ||92|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.93"> kṣīrotthaṃ punarnavanītamutkṛṣṭasnehamādhuryamatiśītaṃ
            saukumāryakaraṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ saṅgrāhi raktapittanetrarogaharaṃ prasādanaṃ ca
            ||93|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.94"> santānikā punarvātaghnī tarpaṇī vṛṣyā balyā snigdhā
            rucyā madhurā madhuravipākā raktapittaprasādanī gurvī ca ||94|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.95"> vikalpa eṣa dadhyādiḥ śreṣṭho gavyo 'bhivarṇitaḥ |
            vikalpānavaśiṣṭāṃs tu kṣīravīryātsam ādiśet ||95|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.96">iti takravargaḥ | atha ghṛtam | ghṛtaṃ tu madhuraṃ
            saumyaṃ mṛdu śītavīryamanabhiṣyandi
            snehanamudāvartonmādāpasmāraśūlajvarānāhavātapittapraśamanamagnidīpanaṃ
            smṛtimatimedhākāntisvaralāvaṇyasaukumāryaujastejobalakaramāyuṣyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ
            medhyaṃ vayaḥsthāpanaṃ guru cakṣuṣyaṃ śleṣmābhivardhanaṃ
            pāpmālakṣmīpraśamanaṃ viṣaharaṃ rakṣoghnaṃ ca ||96|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.97"> vipāke madhuraṃ śītaṃ vātapittaviṣāpaham |
            cakṣuṣyamagryaṃ balyaṃ ca gavyaṃ sarpirguṇottaram ||97|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.98"> ājaṃ ghṛtaṃ dīpanīyaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ balavardhanam | kāse
            śvāse kṣaye cāpi pathyaṃ pāke ca tallaghu ||98|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.99"> madhuraṃ raktapittaghnaṃ guru pāke kaphāvaham |
            vātapittapraśamanaṃ suśītaṃ māhiṣaṃ ghṛtam ||99|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.100"> auṣṭraṃ kaṭu ghṛtaṃ pāke śophakrimiviṣāpaham | dīpanaṃ
            kaphavātaghnaṃ kuṣṭhagulmodarāpaham ||100|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.101"> pāke laghvāvikaṃ sarpirna ca pittaprakopaṇam |
            kaphe 'nile yonidoṣe śoṣe kampe ca taddhitam ||101|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.102"> pāke laghūṣṇavīryaṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ kaphanāśanam | dīpanaṃ
            baddhamūtraṃ ca vidyādaikaśaphaṃ ghṛtam ||102|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.103"> cakṣuṣyamagryaṃ strīṇāṃ tu sarpiḥ syādamṛtopamam |
            vṛddhiṃ karoti dehāgnyor laghupākaṃ viṣāpaham ||103|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.104"> kaṣāyaṃ baddhaviṇmūtraṃ tiktamagnikaraṃ laghu | hanti
            kāreṇavaṃ sarpiḥ kaphakuṣṭhaviṣakrimīn ||104|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.105"> kṣīraghṛtaṃ punaḥ saṅgrāhi
            raktapittabhramamūrcchāpraśamanaṃ netrarogahitaṃ ca ||105|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.106"> sarpirmaṇḍas tu madhuraḥ saro yoniśrotrākṣiśirasāṃ
            śūlaghno bastinasyākṣipūraṇeṣūpadiśyate ||106|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.107"> sarpiḥ purāṇaṃ saraṃ kaṭuvipākaṃ tridoṣāpahaṃ
            mūrcchāmadonmādodarajvaragaraśoṣāpasmārayoniśrotrākṣiśira śūlaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ
            bastinasyapūraṇeṣūpadiśyate ||107|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.108"> bhavati cātra- purāṇaṃ timiraśvāsapīnasajvarakāsanut |
            mūrcchākuṣṭhaviṣonmādagrahāpasmāranāśanam ||108|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.109"> (ekādaśaśataṃ caiva vatsarānuṣitaṃ ghṛtam | rakṣoghnaṃ
            kumbhasarpiḥ syāt paratas tu mahāghṛtam ||109||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.110"> peyaṃ mahāghṛtaṃ bhūtaiḥ kaphaghnaṃ pavanādhikaiḥ |
            balyaṃ pavitraṃ medhyaṃ ca viśeṣāttimirāpaham ||110|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.111"> sarvabhūtaharaṃ caiva ghṛtametat praśasyate)
            ||111||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.112"> iti ghṛtavargaḥ | atha tailāni | tailaṃ tvāgneyamuṣṇaṃ
            tīkṣṇaṃ madhuraṃ madhuravipākaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ prīṇanaṃ vyavāyi sūkṣmaṃ viśadaṃ
            guru saraṃ vikāsi vṛṣyaṃ tvakprasādanaṃ
            medhāmārdavamāṃsasthairyavarṇabalakaraṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ baddhamūtraṃ lekhanaṃ
            tiktakaṣāyānurasaṃ pācanamanilabalāsakṣayakaraṃ krimighnamaśitapittajananaṃ
            yoniśiraḥkarṇaśūlapraśamanaṃ garbhāśayaśodhanaṃ ca, tathā
            chinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭacyutamathitakṣatapiccitabhagnasphuṭitakṣārāgnidagdhaviśliṣṭadāritā
            bhihatadurbhagnamṛgavyālavidaṣṭaprabhṛtiṣu ca pariṣekābhyaṅgāvagāhādiṣu
            tilatailaṃ praśasyate ||112|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.113"> tadbastiṣu ca pāneṣu nasye karṇākṣipūraṇe |
            annapānavidhau cāpi prayojyaṃ vātaśāntaye ||113|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.114"> eraṇḍatailaṃ madhuramuṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ dīpanaṃ kaṭu
            kaṣāyānurasaṃ sūkṣmaṃ srotoviśodhanaṃ tvacyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ madhuravipākaṃ
            vayaḥsthāpanaṃ yoniśukraviśodhanamārogyamedhākāntismṛtibalakaraṃ
            vātakaphaharamadhobhāgadoṣaharaṃ ca ||114|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.115">
            nimbātasīkusumbhamūlakajīmūtakavṛkṣakakṛtavedhanārkakampillakahastikarṇapṛthvīkāpīlu-
            karañjeṅgudīśigrusarṣapasuvarcalāviḍaṅgajyotiṣmatīphalatailāni tīkṣṇāni
            laghūnyuṣṇavīryāṇi kaṭūni kaṭuvipākāni
            sarāṇyanilakaphakṛmikuṣṭhapramehaśirorogāpaharāṇi ceti ||115|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.116"> vātaghnaṃ madhuraṃ teṣu kṣaumaṃ tailaṃ balāpaham |
            kaṭupākamacakṣuṣyaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ gurupittalam ||116|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.117"> kṛmighnaṃ sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ kaṇḍūkuṣṭhāpahaṃ laghu |
            kaphamedonilaharaṃ lekhanaṃ kaṭu dīpanam ||117||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.118"> kṛmighnamiṅgudītailamīṣattiktaṃ tathā laghu |
            kuṣṭhāmayakṛmiharaṃ dṛṣṭiśukrabalāpaham ||118|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.119"> vipāke kaṭukaṃ tailaṃ kausumbhaṃ sarvadoṣakṛt |
            raktapittakaraṃ tīkṣṇamacakṣuṣyaṃ vidāhi ca ||119|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.120">
            kirātatiktakātimuktakabibhītakanālikerakolākṣoḍajīvantīpriyālakarbudāra-
            sūryavallītrapusair vārukakarkārukūṣmāṇḍaprabhṛtīnāṃ tailāni madhurāṇi
            madhuravipākāni vātapittapraśamanāni śītavīryāṇyabhiṣyandīni
            sṛṣṭamūtrāṇyagnisādanāni ceti ||120|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.121"> madhūkakāśmaryapalāśatailāni madhurakaṣāyāṇi
            kaphapittapraśamanāni ||121|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.122"> tuvarakabhallātakataile uṣṇe madhurakaṣāye tiktānurase
            vātakaphakuṣṭhamedomehakṛmipraśamane ubhayatobhāgadoṣahare ca ||122|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.123">
            saraladevadāruśiṃśapāgurugaṇḍīrasārasnehāstiktakaṭukaṣāyā duṣṭavraṇaśodhanāḥ
            kṛmikaphakuṣṭhānilaharāś ca ||123|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.124">
            tumbīkośāmradantīdravantīśyāmāsaptalānīlikākampillakaśaṅkhinīsnehāstiktakaṭukaṣāyā
            adhobhāgadoṣaharāḥ kṛmikaphakuṣṭhānilaharā duṣṭavraṇaśodhanāś ca ||124|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.125"> yavatiktātailaṃ
            sarvadoṣapraśamanamīṣattiktamagnidīpanaṃ lekhanaṃ medhyaṃ pathyaṃ ca ||125|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.126"> ekaiṣikātailaṃ madhuramatiśītaṃ
            pittaharamanilaprakopaṇaṃ śleṣmābhivardhanaṃ ca ||126|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.127"> sahakāratailamīṣattiktamatisugandhi vātakaphaharaṃ
            rūkṣaṃ madhurakaṣāyaṃ rasavannātipittakaraṃ ca ||127|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.128"> phalodbhavāni tailāni yānyuktānīha kānicit | guṇān
            karma ca vijñāya phalānīva vinirdiśet ||128|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.129"> yāvantaḥ sthāvarāḥ snehāḥ samāsātparikīrtitāḥ | sarve
            tailaguṇā jñeyāḥ sarve cānilanāśanāḥ ||129|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.130"> sarvebhyastviha tailebhyastilatailaṃ viśiṣyate |
            niṣpattestadguṇatvāc ca tailatvamitareṣv api ||130|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.131"> grāmyānūpaudakānāṃ ca vasāmedomajjāno gurūṣṇamadhurā
            vātaghnāḥ, jāṅgalaikaśaphakravyādādīnāṃ laghuśītakaṣāyā raktapittaghnāḥ,
            pratudaviṣkirāṇāṃ śleṣmaghnāḥ | tatra ghṛtatailavasāmedomajjāno yathottaraṃ
            guruvipākā vātaharāś ca ||131|| iti tailavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.132"> atha madhuvargaḥ | madhu tu madhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ
            rūkṣaṃ śītamagnidīpanaṃ varṇyaṃ svaryaṃ laghu sukumāraṃ lekhanaṃ hṛdyaṃ
            vājīkaraṇaṃ sandhānaṃ śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ(saṅgrāhi ) cakṣuṣyaṃ prasādanaṃ
            sūkṣmamārgānusāri
            pittaśleṣmamedomehahikkāśvāsakāsātisāraccharditṛṣṇākṛmiviṣapraśamanaṃ hlādi
            tridoṣapraśamanaṃ ca; tat tu laghutvāt kaphaghnaṃ, paicchilyānmādhuryāt
            kaṣāyabhāvāc ca vātapittaghnam ||132|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.133"> pauttikaṃ bhrāmaraṃ kṣaudraṃ mākṣikaṃ chātram eva ca |
            ārghyamauddālakaṃ dālamity aṣṭau madhujātayaḥ ||133|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.134"> viśeṣātpauttikaṃ teṣu rūkṣoṣṇaṃ saviṣānvayāt |
            vātāsṛkpittakṛcchedi vidāhi madakṛnmadhu ||134|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.135">paicchilyāt svādubhūyastvād bhrāmaraṃ gurusañjñitam |
            kṣaudraṃ viśeṣato jñeyaṃ śītalaṃ laghu lekhanam ||135|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.136">tasmāllaghutaraṃ rūkṣaṃ mākṣikaṃ pravaraṃ smṛtam |
            śvāsādiṣu ca rogeṣu praśastaṃ tadviśeṣataḥ ||136|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.137"> svādupākaṃ guru himaṃ picchilaṃ raktapittajit |
            śvitramehakṛmighnaṃ ca vidyācchātraṃ guṇottaram ||137|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.138">ārghyaṃ madhvaticakṣuṣyaṃ kaphapittaharaṃ param |
            kaṣāyaṃ kaṭu pāke ca balyaṃ tiktamavātakṛt ||138|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.139"> auddālakaṃ rucikaraṃ svaryaṃ kuṣṭhaviṣāpaham |
            kaṣāyamamlamuṣṇaṃ ca pittakṛt kaṭupāki ca ||139|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.140.1"> chardimehapraśamanaṃ madhu rūkṣaṃ dalodbhavam |140| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.140.2"> bṛṃhaṇīyaṃ madhu navaṃ nātiśleṣmaharaṃ samam ||140|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.141">medaḥsthaulyāpahaṃ grāhi purāṇamatilekhanam |141|
            doṣatrayaharaṃ pakvamāmamamlaṃ tridoṣakṛt ||141|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.142"> tadyuktaṃ vividhairyogairnihanyādāmayān bahūn |
            nānādravyātmakatvāc ca yogavāhi paraṃ madhu ||142|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.143"> tat tu nānādravyarasaguṇavīryavipākaviruddhānāṃ
            puṣparasānāṃ makṣikāsambhavatvāccānuṣṇopacāram ||143|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.144"> uṣṇairvirudhyate sarvaṃ viṣānvayatayā madhu |
            uṣṇārtamuṣṇair uṣṇe vā tannihanti yathā viṣam ||144|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.145"> tatsaukumāryāc ca tathaiva śaity ānnānauṣadhīnāṃ
            rasasambhavāc ca | uṣṇairvirudhyeta viśeṣataś ca tathā'ntarīkṣeṇa jalena cāpi
            ||145|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.146"> uṣṇena madhu saṃyuktaṃ vamaneṣv avacāritam |
            apākādanavasthānānna virudhyeta pūrvavat ||146|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.147"> madhvāmātparatastvanyadāmaṃ kaṣṭaṃ na vidyate |
            viruddhopakramatvāt tat sarvaṃ hanti yathā viṣam ||147|| iti madhuvargaḥ
            |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.148"> athekṣuvargaḥ | ikṣavo madhurā madhuravipākā guravaḥ
            śītāḥ snigdhā balyā vṛṣyā mūtralā raktapittapraśamanāḥ kṛmikaphakarāśceti |
            te cānekavidhāḥ | tad yathā- ||148|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.149">pauṇḍrako bhīrukaś caiva vaṃśakaḥ śvetaporakaḥ |
            kāntārastāpasekṣuś ca kāṣṭhekṣuḥ sūcipatrakaḥ ||149|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.150"> naipālo dīrghapatraś ca nīlaporo 'tha kośakṛt | ity etā
            jātayaḥ sthaulyād, |.. |150|... guṇān vakṣyāmyataḥ param ||150|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.151"> suśīto madhuraḥ snigdho bṛṃhaṇaḥ śleṣmalaḥ saraḥ |
            avidāhī gururvṛṣyaḥ pauṇḍrako bhīrukas tathā ||151|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.152">ābhyāṃ tulyaguṇaḥ kiñcitsakṣāro vaṃśako mataḥ |
            vaṃśavacchvetaporas tu kiñciduṣṇaḥ sa vātahā ||152|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.153"> kāntāratāpasāvikṣū vaṃśakānugatau matau | evaṅguṇastu
            kāṣṭhekṣuḥ sa tu vātaprakopaṇaḥ ||153|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.154"> sūcīpatro nīlaporau naipālo dīrghapatrakaḥ | vātalāḥ
            kaphapittaghnāḥ sakaṣāyā vidāhinaḥ ||154|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.155"> kośakāro guruḥ śīto raktapittakṣayāpahaḥ |155| atīva
            madhuro mūle madhye madhura eva tu ||155||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.156"> agreṣv akṣiṣu vijñeya ikṣūṇāṃ lavaṇo rasaḥ ||156|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.157"> avidāhī kaphakaro vātapittanivāraṇaḥ | vaktraprahlādano
            vṛṣyo dantaniṣpīḍito rasaḥ ||157|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.158"> gururvidāhī viṣṭambhī yāntrikas tu prakīrtitaḥ |158|
            pakvo guruḥ saraḥ snigdhaḥ satīkṣṇaḥ kaphavātanut ||158|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.159"> phāṇitaṃ guru madhuramabhiṣyandi bṛṃhaṇamavṛṣyaṃ
            tridoṣakṛc ca ||159|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.160"> guḍaḥ sakṣāramadhuro nātiśītaḥ snigdho
            mūtraraktaśodhano nātipittajidvātaghno medaḥkṛmikaphakaro balyo vṛṣyaśca
            ||160|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.161"> pittaghno madhuraḥ śuddho vātaghno 'sṛkprasādanaḥ |161|
            sapurāṇo 'dhikaguṇo guḍaḥ pathyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||161|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.162"> matsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarā vimalajātā uttarottaraṃ śītāḥ
            snigdhāḥ gurutarā madhuratarā vṛṣyā raktapittapraśamanāstṛṣṇāpraśamanāśca
            ||162|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.163"> yathā yathaiṣāṃ vaimalyaṃ madhuratvaṃ tathā tathā |
            snehagauravaśaity āni saratvaṃ ca tathā tathā ||163|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.164"> yo yo matsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarāṇāṃ svako guṇaḥ | tena
            tenaiva nirdeśyas teṣāṃ visrāvaṇo guṇaḥ ||164|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.165"> sārasthitā suvimalā niḥkṣārā ca yathā yathā | tathā
            guṇavatī sarvā vijñeyā śarkarā budhaiḥ ||165|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.166"> madhuśarkarā punaśchardyatīsāraharī rūkṣā chedanī
            prasādanī kaṣāyamadhurā madhuravipākā ca ||166|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.167"> yavāsaśarkarā madhurakaṣāyā tiktānurasā śleṣmaharī sarā
            ceti ||167|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.168"> yāvatyaḥ śarkarāḥ proktāḥ sarvā dāhapraṇāśanāḥ |
            raktapittapraśamanāśchardimūrcchātṛṣāpahāḥ ||168|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.169"> rūkṣaṃ madhūkapuṣpotthaṃ phāṇitaṃ vātapittakṛt |
            kaphaghnaṃ madhuraṃ pāke kaṣāyaṃ bastidūṣaṇam ||169|| itīkṣuvargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.170"> atha madyavargaḥ | sarvaṃ pittakaraṃ madyamamlaṃ
            rocanadīpanam | bhedanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ hṛdyaṃ bastiviśodhanam ||170|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.171"> pāke laghu vidāhyuṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇamindriyabodhanam | vikāsi

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.172"> mārdvīkamavidāhitvānmadhurānvayatas tathā |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.173"> madhuraṃ taddhi rūkṣaṃ ca kaṣāyānurasaṃ laghu |
            laghupāki saraṃ śoṣaviṣamajvaranāśanam ||173||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.174"> mārdvīkālpāntaraṃ kiñcit khārjūraṃ vātakopanam | tadeva

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.175"> kaṣāyamadhuraṃ hṛdyaṃ sugandhīndriyabodhanam |175|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.176"> stanyaraktakṣayahitā surā bṛṃhaṇadīpanī |176|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.178">prasannā kaphavātārśovibandhānāhanāśanī |178|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.179"> rūkṣā nātikaphā vṛṣyā pācanī cākṣikī smṛtā ||179|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.180"> tridoṣo bhedyavṛṣyaś ca kohalo vadanapriyaḥ |180|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.181">hṛdyaḥ pravāhikāṭopadurnāmānilaśoṣahṛt |181| bakkaso

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.182"> dīpanaḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtro viśado 'lpamado guruḥ |182| kaṣāyo

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.183"> śārkaro madhuro rucyo dīpano bastiśodhanaḥ | vātaghno

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.184"> tadvat pakvarasaḥ śīdhurbalavarṇakaraḥ saraḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.185"> karśanaḥ śītarasikaḥ śvayathūdaranāśanaḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.189">tiktaḥ kaṣāyaḥ śophaghnastīkṣṇaḥ svāduravātakṛt |189|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.190"> kṛmimedonilaharo maireyo madhuro guruḥ |190| balyaḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.195"> bahudoṣaharaś caiva doṣāṇāṃ śamanaś ca saḥ | dīpanaḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.196"> śūlādhmānodaraplīhajvarājīrṇārśasāṃ hitaḥ |196|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.197"> cikitsiteṣu vakṣyante 'riṣṭā rogaharāḥ pṛthak |197|
            ariṣṭāsavaśīdhūnāṃ guṇān karmāṇi cādiśet ||197|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.198"> buddhyā yathāsvaṃ saṃskāramavekṣya kuśalo bhiṣak |198|
            sāndraṃ vidāhi durgandhaṃ virasaṃ kṛmilaṃ guru ||198|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.199"> ahṛdyaṃ taruṇaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ durbhājanasthitam |
            alpauṣadhaṃ paryuṣitamatyacchaṃ picchilaṃ ca yat ||199||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.200"> tadvarjyaṃ sarvathā madyaṃ kiñciccheṣaṃ tu yadbhavet |
            tatra yat stokasambhāraṃ taruṇaṃ picchilaṃ guru ||200||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.201"> kaphaprako pi tanmadyaṃ durjaraṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
            pittaprako pi bahalaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ vidāhi ca ||201|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.202">ahṛdyaṃ pelavaṃ pūti kṛmilaṃ virasaṃ ca yat | tathā
            paryuṣitaṃ cāpi vidyādanilakopanam ||202||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.203">sarvadoṣair upetaṃ tu sarvadoṣaprakopaṇam |203|
            cirasthitaṃ jātarasaṃ dīpanaṃ kaphavātajit ||203|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.204">rucyaṃ prasannaṃ surabhi madyaṃ sevyaṃ madāvaham |204|
            tasyānekaprakārasya madyasya rasavīryataḥ ||204|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.205"> saukṣmyādauṣṇyāc ca taikṣṇyāc ca vikāsitvāc ca vahninā
            sametya hṛdayaṃ prāpya dhamanīrūrdhvamāgatam | vicālyendriyacetāṃsi vīryaṃ
            madayate 'cirāt ||205||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.206"> cireṇa ślaiṣmike puṃsi pānato jāyate madaḥ |
            acirādvātike dṛṣṭaḥ, paittike śīghram eva ca ||206|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.207"> sāttvike śaucadākṣiṇyaharṣamaṇḍanalālasaḥ |
            gītādhyayanasaubhāgyasuratotsāhakṛnmadaḥ ||207|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.208">rājase duḥkhaśīlatvamātmatyāgaṃ sasāhasam | kalahaṃ
            sānubandhaṃ tu karoti puruṣe madaḥ ||208|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.209"> aśaucanidrāmātsaryāgamyāgamanalolatāḥ | asatyabhāṣaṇaṃ
            cāpi kuryād dhi tāmase madaḥ ||209|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.210"> raktapittakaraṃ śuktaṃ chedanaṃ bhuktapācanam |
            vaisvaryaṃ jaraṇaṃ śleṣmapāṇḍukrimiharaṃ laghu ||210|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.211">tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ mūtralaṃ hṛdyaṃ kaphaghnaṃ kaṭupāki ca |211|
            tadvattadāsutaṃ sarvaṃ rocanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||211|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.212"> gauḍāni rasaśuktāni madhuśuktāni yāni ca | yathāpūrvaṃ
            gurutarāṇyabhiṣyandakarāṇi ca ||212|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.213"> tuṣāmbu dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ hṛtpāṇḍukṛmiroganut |
            grahaṇyarśovikāraghnaṃ bhedi sauvīrakaṃ tathā ||213|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.214"> dhānyāmlaṃ dhānyayonitvājjīvanaṃ dāhanāśanam | sparśāt
            pānāt tu pavanakaphatṛṣṇāharaṃ laghu ||214|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.215"> taikṣṇyāc ca nirharedāśu kaphaṃ gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇāt |
            mukhavairasyadaurgandhyamalaśoṣaklamāpaham ||215|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.216">dīpanaṃ jaraṇaṃ bhedi hitamāsthāpaneṣu ca |
            samudramāśritānāṃ ca janānāṃ sātmyamucyate ||216|| iti madhyavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.217"> atha mūtrāṇi | mūtrāṇi
            gomahiṣyajāvigajahayakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ tīkṣṇānyuṣṇāni kaṭūni tiktāni
            lavaṇānurasāni laghūni śodhanāni
            kaphavātakṛmimedoviṣagulmārśadarakuṣṭhaśophārocakapāṇḍurogaharāṇi hṛdyāni
            dīpanāni ca sāmānyataḥ ||217|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.218">bhavataś cātra- tat sarvaṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ
            laghu | śodhanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ kṛmimedoviṣāpaham ||218|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.219"> arśojaṭharagulmaghnaṃ śophārocakanāśanam |
            pāṇḍurogaharaṃ bhedi hṛdyaṃ dīpanapācanam ||219|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.220"> gomūtraṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ sakṣāratvānna vātalam |
            laghvagnidīpanaṃ medhyaṃ pittalaṃ kaphavātanut ||220|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.221"> śūlagulmodarānāhavirekāsthāpanādiṣu |
            mūtraprayogasādhyeṣu gavyaṃ mūtraṃ prayojayet ||221|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.222"> durnāmodaraśūleṣu kuṣṭhamehāviśuddhiṣu |
            ānāhaśophagulmeṣu pāṇḍuroge ca māhiṣam ||222|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.223"> kāsaśvāsāpahaṃ śophakāmalāpāṇḍuroganut |
            kaṭutiktānvitaṃ chāgamīṣanmārutakopanam ||223|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.224"> kāsaplīhodaraśvāsaśoṣavarcograhe hitam | sakṣāraṃ
            tiktakaṭukamuṣṇaṃ vātaghnamāvikam ||224|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.225"> dīpanaṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ vātacetovikāranut | āśvaṃ
            kaphaharaṃ mūtraṃ kṛmidadruṣu śasyate ||225|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.226"> satiktaṃ lavaṇaṃ bhedi vātaghnaṃ pittakopanam | tīkṣṇaṃ
            kṣāre kilāse ca nāgaṃ mūtraṃ prayojayet ||226|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.227"> garacetovikāraghnaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ grahaṇiroganut | dīpanaṃ
            gārdabhaṃ mūtraṃ kṛmivātakaphāpaham ||227|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.228"> śophakuṣṭhodaronmādamārutakrimināśanam | arśoghnaṃ
            kārabhaṃ mūtraṃ... |228| |.. mānuṣaṃ ca viṣāpaham ||228|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.229"> dravadravyāṇi sarvāṇi samāsāt kīrtitāni tu |
            kāladeśavibhāgajño nṛpaterdātumarhati ||229|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
            dravadravyavijñānīyo nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||45|| </l>
        </div>
        <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3"> dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca- prāgabhihitaḥ
            ‘prāṇināṃ punarmūlamāhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca, sa ṣaṭsu raseṣvāyattaḥ, rasāḥ
            punardravyāśrayiṇaḥ,’ dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī
            doṣāṇāṃ sāmyaṃ ca, brahmāderapi ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthity utpattivināśahetuḥ,
            āhārādevābhivṛddhirbalamārogyaṃ varṇendriyaprasādaśca, tathā
            hyāhāravaiṣamyādasvāsthyaṃ; tasyāśitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
            nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpasyānekavidhaprabhāvasya pṛthak
            pṛthagdravyarasaguṇavīryavipākakarmāṇīcchāmi jñātuṃ, na
            hy anavabuddhasvabhāvā bhiṣajaḥ svasthānuvṛttiṃ roganigrahaṇaṃ ca kartuṃ
            samarthāḥ; āhārāyattāś ca sarvaprāṇino yasmāttasmād annapānavidhim upadiśatu me
            bhagavānity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ- atha khalu vatsa suśruta!
            yathāpraśnamucyamānam upadhārayasva- ||3|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4"> tatra,
            lohitaśālikalamakardamakapāṇḍukasugandhakaśakunāhṛtapuṣpāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukarodhrapuṣpaka-
            dīrghaśūkakāñcanakamahiṣamahāśūkahāyanakadūṣakamahādūṣakaprabhṛtayaḥ śālayaḥ
            ||4|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5"> madhurā vīryataḥ śītā laghupākā balāvahāḥ |
            pittaghnālpānilakaphāḥ snigdhā baddhālpavarcasaḥ ||5|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6"> teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ |
            cakṣuṣyo varṇabalakṛt svaryo hṛdyastṛṣāpahaḥ ||6|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7"> vraṇyo jvaraharaś caiva sarvadoṣaviṣāpahaḥ |7|
            tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo 'varāḥ ||7|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8">
            ṣaṣṭikakāṅgukamukundakapītakapramodakakākalakāsanapuṣpakamahāṣaṣṭikacūrṇakakuravakakedāraprabhṛtayaḥ
            ṣaṣṭikāḥ ||8|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9"> rase pāke ca madhurāḥ śamanā vātapittayoḥ | śālīnāṃ ca
            guṇaistulyā bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphaśukralāḥ ||9|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10"> ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravaras teṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | mṛduḥ
            snigdhastridoṣaghnaḥ sthairyakṛdbalavardhanaḥ ||10|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11"> vipāke madhuro grāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ |11|
            śeṣāstvalpāntarāstasmāt ṣaṣṭikāḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ ||11|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12">
            kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhajatumukhanandīmukhalāvākṣakatvaritakakukkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalaprabhṛtayo
            vrīhayaḥ ||12|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke 'madhurā vīryato 'himāḥ |
            alpābhiṣyandinastulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikairbaddhavarcasaḥ ||13|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14"> kṛṣṇavrīhirvaras teṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
            tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśo vrīhayo 'pare ||14|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15"> dagdhāyāmavanau jātāḥ śālayo laghupākinaḥ | kaṣāyā
            baddhaviṇmūtrā rūkṣāḥ śleṣmāpakarṣaṇāḥ ||15|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.16"> sthalajāḥ kaphapittaghnāḥ kaṣāyāḥ kaṭukānvayāḥ |
            kiñcitsatiktamadhurāḥ pavanānalavardhanāḥ ||16|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.17"> kaidārā madhurā vṛṣyā balyāḥ pittanibarhaṇāḥ |
            īṣatkaṣāyālpamalā guravaḥ kaphaśukralāḥ ||17|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.18"> ropyātiropyā laghavaḥ śīghrapākā guṇottarāḥ | adāhino
            doṣaharā balyā mūtravivardhanāḥ ||18|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.19"> śālayaśchinnarūḍhā ye rūkṣāste baddhavarcasaḥ | tiktāḥ
            kaṣāyāḥ pittaghnā laghupākāḥ kaphāpahāḥ ||19|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.20"> vistareṇāyamuddiṣṭaḥ śālivargo hitāhitaḥ |20| iti
            śālivargaḥ | atha kudhānyavargaḥ | tadvat kudhānyamudgādimāṣādīnāṃ ca
            vakṣyate ||20|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.21">
            koradūṣakaśyāmākanīvāraśāntanuvarakoddālakapriyaṅgumadhūlikānandīmukhī-
            kuruvindagavedhukasarabarukatoda(ya)parṇīmukundakaveṇuyavaprabhṛtayaḥ
            kudhānyaviśeṣāḥ ||21|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.22"> uṣṇāḥ kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ | śleṣmaghnā
            baddhanisyandā vātapittaprakopaṇāḥ ||22|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.23"> kaṣāyamadhuras teṣāṃ śītaḥ pittāpahaḥ smṛtaḥ | kodravaśca
            sanīvāraḥ śyāmākaś ca saśāntanuḥ ||23|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.24"> kṛṣṇā raktāś ca pītāś ca śvetāś caiva priyaṅgavaḥ |
            yathottaraṃ pradhānāḥ syū rūkṣāḥ kaphaharāḥ smṛtāḥ ||24|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.25"> madhūlī madhurā śītā snigdhā nandīmukhī tathā |25|
            viśoṣī tatra bhūyiṣṭhaṃ varukaḥ samukundakaḥ ||25|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.26"> rūkṣā veṇuyavā jñeyā vīryoṣṇā kaṭupākinaḥ | baddhamūtrāḥ
            kaphaharāḥ kaṣāyā vātakopanāḥ ||26|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.27">
            mudgavanamudgakalāyamakuṣṭhamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakasatīnatripuṭakahareṇvāḍhakīprabhṛtayo
            vaidalāḥ ||27|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.28"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītāḥ kaṭupākā marutkarāḥ |
            baddhamūtrapurīṣāś ca pittaśleṣmaharās tathā ||28|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.29"> nātyarthaṃ vātalāsteṣu mudgā dṛṣṭiprasādanāḥ | pradhānā
            haritās tatra vanyā mudgasamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||29|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.30"> vipāke madhurāḥ proktā masūrā baddhavarcasaḥ |30|
            makuṣṭhakāḥ kṛmikarāḥ... |30| |.. kalāyāḥ pracurānilāḥ ||30|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.31"> āḍhakī kaphapittaghnī nātivātaprakopaṇī |31| vātalāḥ
            śītamadhurāḥ sakaṣāyā virūkṣaṇāḥ ||31|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.32">kaphaśoṇitapittaghnāścaṇakāḥ puṃstvanāśanāḥ | ta eva
            ghṛtasaṃyuktāstridoṣaśamanāḥ param ||32|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.33"> hareṇavaḥ satīnāś ca vijñeyā baddhavarcasaḥ |33| ṛte
            mudgamasūrābhyāmanye tvād hmānakārakāḥ ||33|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34"> māṣo gururbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdhoṣṇavṛṣyo
            madhuro 'nilaghnaḥ | santarpaṇaḥ stanyakaro viśeṣādbalapradaḥ
            śukrakaphāvahaś ca ||34|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35"> kaṣāyabhāvānna purīṣabhedī na mūtralo naiva kaphasya
            kartā | svādurvipāke madhuro 'lasāndraḥ santarpaṇaḥ stanyarucipradaś ca ||35|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36"> māṣaiḥ samānaṃ phalamātmaguptamuktaṃ ca kākāṇḍaphalaṃ
            tathaiva |36| āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaś ca ||36|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37"> uṣṇaḥ kulattho rasataḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭurvipāke
            kaphamārutaghnaḥ | śukrāśmarīgulmaniṣūdanaś ca sāṅgrāhikaḥ pīnasakāsahantā
            ||37|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38"> ānāhamedogudakīlahikkāśvāsāpahaḥ śoṇitapittakṛc ca |
            kaphasya hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ ||38|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39"> īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ satiktaḥ sāṅgrāhikaḥ
            pittakarastathoṣṇaḥ | tilo vipāke madhuro baliṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇe lepana eva
            pathyaḥ ||39|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40"> dantyo 'gnimedhājanano 'lpamūtrastvacyo 'tha keśyo 'nilahā
            guruś ca |40| tileṣu sarveṣv asitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarāstathā'nye
            ||40|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41"> yavaḥ kaṣāyo madhuro himaś ca kaṭurvipāke kaphapittahārī
            | vraṇeṣu pathyastilavac ca nityaṃ prabaddhamūtro bahuvātavarcāḥ ||41|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42">sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇakṛc ca sapicchilaḥ
            sthūlavilekhanaś ca | medomaruttṛḍ.hharaṇo 'tirūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ
            śoṇitapittayoś ca ||42|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43"> ebhir guṇairhīnataraistu
            kiñcidvidyādyavebhyo 'tiyavānaśeṣaiḥ |43| godhūma ukto madhuro guruś ca balyaḥ
            sthiraḥ śukrarucipradaś ca ||43|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44">snigdho 'tiśīto 'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛcchleṣmakaraḥ
            saraś ca |44| rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśoṣaśukrabalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī ||44|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45"> kaṭurvipāke madhuras tu śimbaḥ
            prabhinnaviṇmārutapittalaś ca |45| sitāsitāḥ pītakaraktavarṇā bhavanti
            ye 'nekavidhās tu śimbāḥ ||45|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46"> yathāditaste guṇataḥ pradhānā jñeyāḥ kaṭūṣṇā
            rasapākayoś ca |46| sahādvayaṃ mūlakajāś ca śimbāḥ kuśimbivallīprabhavāstu
            śimbāḥ ||46|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47"> jñeyā vipāke madhurā rase ca balapradāḥ
            pittanibarhaṇāś ca |47| vidāhavantaś ca bhṛśaṃ virūkṣā viṣṭabhya
            jīryantyanilapradāś ca ||47|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48"> rucipradāś caiva sudurjarāś ca sarve smṛtā vaidalikāstu
            śimbāḥ |48| kaṭurvipāke kaṭukaḥ kaphaghno vidāhibhāvādahitaḥ kusumbhaḥ
            ||48|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49"> uṣṇā'tasī svādurasā'nilaghnī pittolbaṇā syāt kaṭukā
            vipāke | pāke rase cāpi kaṭuḥ pradiṣṭaḥ siddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī
            ||49||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.50">tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣaḥ
            kaphamārutaghnastathāguṇaś cāsitasarṣapo 'pi |50| anārtavaṃ
            vyādhihatamaparyāgatam eva ca | abhūmijaṃ navaṃ cāpi na dhānyaṃ guṇavat
            smṛtam ||50|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.51"> navaṃ dhānyamabhiṣyandi laghu saṃvatsaroṣitam |51|
            vidāhi guru viṣṭambhi virūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭidūṣaṇam ||51|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52"> śālyādeḥ sarṣapāntasya vividhasyāsya bhāgaśaḥ |
            kālapramāṇasaṃskāramātrāḥ samparikīrtitāḥ ||52|| iti kudhānyavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53"> atha māṃsavargaḥ | ata ūrdhvaṃ māṃsavargānupadekṣyāmaḥ;
            tad yathā- jaleśayā, ānūpā, grāmyāḥ, kravyabhuja, ekaśaphā, jāṅgalāśceti
            ṣaṇmāṃsavargā bhavanti | eteṣāṃ vargāṇāmuttarottarā pradhānatamāḥ | te
            punardvividhā jāṅgalā ānūpāśceti | tatra jāṅgalavargo 'ṣṭavidhaḥ | tad yathā-
            jaṅghālā, viṣkirāḥ, pratudā, guhāśayāḥ, prasahāḥ, parṇamṛgā, bileśayā,
            grāmyāśceti | teṣāṃ jaṅghālaviṣkirau pradhānatamau ||53|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54">
            tāveṇahariṇarkṣakuraṅgakarālakṛtamālaśarabhaśvadaṃṣṭrāpṛṣatacāruṣkaramṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayo
            jaṅghālā mṛgāḥ kaṣāyā madhurā laghavo vātapittaharāstīkṣṇā hṛdyā
            bastiśodhanāś ca ||54|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55"> kaṣāyamadhuro hṛdyaḥ pittāsṛkkapharogahā | saṅgrāhī
            rocano balyas teṣāṃ eṇo jvarāpahaḥ ||55|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56"> madhuro madhuraḥ pāke doṣaghno 'naladīpanaḥ | śītalo
            baddhaviṇmūtra sugandhirhariṇo laghuḥ ||56|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.57"> eṇaḥ kṛṣṇastayor jñeyo hariṇastāmra ucyate | yo na kṛṣṇo
            na tāmraś ca kuraṅgaḥ so 'bhidhīyate ||57|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.58"> śītā'sṛkpittaśamanī vijñeyā mṛgamātṛkā |
            sannipātakṣayaśvāsakāsahikkārucipraṇut ||58|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.59">
            lāvatittirikapiñjalavartīravartikāvartakanaptṛkāvārtīkacakorakalaviṅkamayūrakrakaropacakra-
            kukkuṭasāraṅgaśatapatrakutittirikuruvāhakayavālakaprabhṛtayastryāhalā
            viṣkirāḥ ||59|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60"> laghavaḥ śītamadhurāḥ kaṣāyā doṣanāśanāḥ |60| saṅgrāhī
            dīpanaś caiva kaṣāyamadhuro laghuḥ | lāvaḥ kaṭuvipākaś ca sannipāte tu pūjitaḥ
            ||60|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.61"> īṣadgurūṣṇamadhuro vṛṣyo medhāgnivardhanaḥ | tittiriḥ
            sarvadoṣaghno grāhī varṇaprasādanaḥ ||61|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.62"> raktapittaharaḥ śīto laghuś cāpi kapiñjalaḥ | kaphottheṣu
            ca rogeṣu mandavāte ca śasyate ||62||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.63"> hikkāśvāsānilaharo viśeṣād gauratittiriḥ |63|
            vātapittaharā vṛṣyā medhāgnibalavardhanāḥ ||63|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.64"> laghavaḥ krakarā hṛdyās tathā caivopacakrakāḥ |64|
            kaṣāyaḥ svādulavaṇastvacyaḥ keśyo 'rucau hitaḥ ||64|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.65">mayūraḥ svaramedhāgnidṛkśrotrendriyadārḍhyakṛt |65|
            snigdhoṣṇo 'nilahā vṛṣyaḥ svedasvarabalāvahaḥ ||65|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.66">bṛṃhaṇaḥ kukkuṭo vanyastadvadgrāmyo gurus tu saḥ |
            vātarogakṣayavamīviṣamajvaranāśanaḥ ||66|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.67">
            kapotapārāvatabhṛṅgarājaparabhṛtakoyaṣṭikakuliṅgagṛhakuliṅgagokṣveḍakaḍiṇḍimāṇavakaśatapatraka-
            mātṛnindakabhedāśiśukasārikāvalgulīgiriśālaṭvālaṭṭūṣakasugṛhākhañjarīṭahārītadātyūhaprabhṛtayaḥ
            , pratudāḥ ||67|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.68"> kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ phalāhārā marutkarāḥ |
            pittaśleṣmaharāḥ śītā baddhamūtrālpavarcasaḥ ||68|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.69"> sarvadoṣakaras teṣāṃ bhedāśī maladūṣakaḥ |69|
            kaṣāyasvādulavaṇo guruḥ kāṇakapotakaḥ ||69|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.70"> raktapittapraśamanaḥ kaṣāyaviśado 'pi ca | vipāke
            madhuraś cāpi guruḥ pārāvataḥ smṛtaḥ ||70|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.71"> kuliṅgo madhuraḥ snigdhaḥ kaphaśukravivardhanaḥ |71|
            raktapittaharo veśmakuliṅgastvatiśukralaḥ ||71|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.72">
            siṃhavyāghravṛkatarakṣvṛkṣadvīpimārjāraśṛgālamṛgervārukaprabhṛtayo guhāśayāḥ
            ||72|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.73"> madhurā guravaḥ snigdhā balyā mārutanāśanāḥ | uṣṇavīryā
            hitā nityaṃ netraguhyavikāriṇām ||73|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.74">
            kākakaṅkakuraracāṣabhāsaśaśaghātyulūkacilliśyenagṛdhraprabhṛtayaḥ prasahāḥ
            ||74|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.75"> ete siṃhādibhiḥ sarve samānā vāyasādayaḥ |
            rasavīryavipākeṣu viśeṣācchoṣiṇe hitāḥ ||75|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.76"> madgumūṣikavṛkṣaśāyikāvakuśapūtighāsavānaraprabhṛtayaḥ
            parṇamṛgāḥ ||76|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.77"> madhurā guravo vṛṣyāścakṣuṣyāḥ śoṣiṇe hitāḥ |
            sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāś ca kāsārśaḥśvāsanāśanāḥ ||77|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.78">
            śvāvicchalyakagodhāśaśavṛṣadaṃśalopākalomaśakarṇakadalīmṛgapriyakājagarasarpamūṣikanakulamahābabhruprabhṛtayo
            bileśayāḥ ||78|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.79"> varcomūtraṃ saṃhataṃ kuryurete vīrye coṣṇāḥ pūrvavat
            svādupākāḥ | vātaṃ hanyuḥ śleṣmapitte ca kuryuḥ snigdhāḥ
            kāsaśvāsakārśyāpahāś ca ||79|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.80"> kaṣāyamadhuras teṣāṃ śaśaḥ pittakaphāpahaḥ |
            nātiśītalavīryatvād vātasādhāraṇo mataḥ ||80|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.81"> godhā vipāke madhurā kaṣāyakaṭukā smṛtā |
            vātapittapraśamanī bṛṃhaṇī balavardhanī ||81|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.82"> śalyakaḥ svādupittaghno laghuḥ śīto viṣāpahaḥ | priyako
            mārute pathyo 'jagarastvarśasāṃ hitaḥ ||82|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.83"> durnāmāniladoṣaghnāḥ kṛmidūṣīviṣāpahāḥ | cakṣuṣyā
            madhurāḥ pāke sarpā medhāgnivardhanāḥ ||83|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.84"> darvīkarā dīpakāś ca teṣūktāḥ kaṭupākinaḥ |
            madhurāś cāticakṣuṣyāḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtramārutāḥ ||84|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.85"> aśvāśvataragokharoṣṭrabastorabhramedaḥpucchakaprabhṛtayo
            grāmyāḥ ||85|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.86"> grāmyā vātaharāḥ sarve bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphapittalāḥ | madhurā
            rasapākābhyāṃ dīpanā balavardhanāḥ ||86|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.87"> nātiśīto guruḥ snigdho mandapittakaphaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            chagalastvanabhiṣyandī teṣāṃ pīnasanāśanaḥ ||87|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.88"> bṛṃhaṇaṃ māṃsamaurabhraṃ pittaśleṣmāvahaṃ guru |88|
            medaḥpucchodbhavaṃ vṛṣyamaurabhrasadṛśaṃ guṇaiḥ ||88|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.89"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyaviṣamajvaranāśanam | śramātyagnihitaṃ
            gavyaṃ pavitramanilāpaham ||89|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.90"> aurabhravatsalavaṇaṃ māṃsamekaśaphodbhavam |90|
            alpābhiṣyandyayaṃ vargo jāṅgalaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ||90|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.91"> dūre janāntanilayā dūre pānīyagocarāḥ | ye mṛgāśca
            vihaṅgāś ca te 'lpābhiṣyandino matāḥ ||91|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.92"> atīvāsannanilayāḥ samīpodakagocarāḥ | ye mṛgāśca
            vihaṅgāś ca mahābhiṣyandinas tu te ||92||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.93"> ānūpavargas tu pañcavidhaḥ | tad yathā- kūlacarāḥ, plavāḥ,
            koṣasthāḥ, pādino, matsyāś ceti ||93|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.94"> tatra
            gajagavayamahiṣarurucamarasṛmararohitavarāhakhaḍgigokarṇakālapucchakodranyaṅkvaraṇyagavayaprabhṛtayaḥ
            kūlacarāḥ paśavaḥ ||94|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.95"> vātapittaharā vṛṣyā madhurā rasapākayoḥ | śītalā balinaḥ
            snigdhā mūtralāḥ kaphavardhanaḥ ||95|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.96"> virūkṣaṇo lekhanaś ca vīryoṣṇaḥ pittadūṣaṇaḥ |
            svādvamlalavaṇas teṣāṃ gajaḥ śleṣmānilāpahaḥ ||96||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.97"> gavayasya tu māṃsaṃ hi snigdhaṃ madhurakāsajit | vipāke
            madhuraṃ cāpi vyavāyasya tu vardhanam ||97|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.98"> snigdhoṣṇamadhuro vṛṣyo mahiṣastarpaṇo guruḥ |
            nidrāpuṃstvabalastanyavardhano māṃsadārḍhyakṛt ||98|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.99"> rurormāṃsaṃ samadhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ smṛtam |
            vātapittopaśamanaṃ guru śukravivardhanam ||99|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.100">tathā camaramāṃsaṃ tu snigdhaṃ madhurakāsajit | vipāke
            madhuraṃ cāpi vātapittapraṇāśanam ||100|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.101"> sṛmarasya tu māṃsaṃ ca kaṣāyānurasaṃ smṛtam |
            vātapittopaśamanaṃ guru śukravivardhanam ||101|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.102">svedanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vṛṣyaṃ śītalaṃ tarpaṇaṃ guru |
            śramānilaharaṃ snigdhaṃ vārāhaṃ balavardhanam ||102|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.103"> kaphaghnaṃ khaḍgipiśitaṃ kaṣāyamanilāpaham | pitryaṃ
            pavitramāyuṣyaṃ baddhamūtraṃ virūkṣaṇam ||103|| g </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.104">okarṇamāṃsaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ mṛdu kaphāvaham | vipāke
            madhuraṃ cāpi raktapittavināśanam ||104|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.105">
            haṃsasārasakrauñcacakravākakurarakādambakāraṇḍavajīvañjīvakabakabalākāpuṇḍarīkaplavaśarārīmukha-
            nandīmukhamadgūtkrośakācākṣamallikākṣaśuklākṣapuṣkaraśāyikākonālakāmbukukkuṭikāmegharāvaśvetavāralaprabhṛtayaḥ
            plavāḥ saṅghātacāriṇaḥ ||105|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.106"> raktapittaharāḥ śītāḥ snigdhā vṛṣyā marujjitaḥ |
            sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāś ca madhurā rasapākayoḥ ||106|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.107"> gurūṣṇamadhuraḥ snigdhaḥ svaravarṇabalapradaḥ |
            bṛṃhaṇaḥ śukralas teṣāṃ haṃso vātavikāranut ||107|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.108"> śaṅkhaśaṅkhanakaśuktiśambūkabhallūkaprabhṛtayaḥ
            kośasthāḥ ||108|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.109"> kūrmakumbhīrakarkaṭakakṛṣṇakarkaṭakaśiśumāraprabhṛtayaḥ
            pādinaḥ ||109|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.110"> śaṅkhakūrmādayaḥ svādurasapākā marunnudaḥ | śītāḥ
            snigdhā hitāḥ pitte varcasyāḥ śleṣmavardhanāḥ ||110|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.111"> kṛṣṇakarkaṭakas teṣāṃ balyaḥ koṣṇo 'nilāpahaḥ | śuklaḥ
            sandhānakṛt sṛṣṭaviṇmūtro 'nilapittahā ||111|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.112"> matsyās tu dvividhā nādeyāḥ sāmudrāś ca ||112|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.113"> tatra nādeyāḥ-
            rohitapāṭhīnapāṭalārājīvavarmigomatsyakṛṣṇamatsyavāguñjāramuralasahasradaṃṣṭraprabhṛtayaḥ
            ||113|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.114"> nādeyā madhurā matsyā guravo mārutāpahāḥ |
            raktapittakarāścoṣṇā vṛṣyāḥ snigdhālpavarcasaḥ ||114|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.115"> kaṣāyānurasas teṣāṃ śaṣpaśaivālabhojanaḥ | rohito
            mārutaharo nātyarthaṃ pittakopanaḥ ||115|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.116"> pāṭhīnaḥ śleṣmalo vṛṣyo nidrāluḥ piśitāśanaḥ |
            dūṣayed raktapittaṃ tu kuṣṭharogaṃ karotyasau | muralo bṛṃhaṇo vṛṣyaḥ
            stanyaśleṣmakaras tathā ||116|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.117"> sarastaḍāgasambhūtāḥ snigdhāḥ svādurasāḥ smṛtāḥ |
            mahāhradeṣu balinaḥ, svalpe 'mbhasyabalāḥ smṛtāḥ ||117|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.118">
            timitimiṅgilakuliśapākamatsyanirulanandivāra(ru)lakamakaragargaracandrakamahāmīnarājīvaprabhṛtayaḥ
            sāmudrāḥ ||118|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.119"> sāmudrā guravaḥ snigdhā madhurā nātipittalāḥ | uṣṇā
            vātaharā vṛṣyā varcasyāḥ śleṣmavardhanāḥ ||119|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.120"> balāvahā viśeṣeṇa māṃsāśitvāt samudrajāḥ |120|
            samudrajebhyo nādeyā bṛṃhaṇatvād guṇottarāḥ ||120|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.121">teṣāmapyanilaghnatvāccauṇṭyakaupyau guṇottarau |
            snigdhatvāt svādupākatvāt tayor vāpy ā guṇādhikāḥ ||121|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.122"> nādeyā guravo madhye yasmāt pucchāsyacāriṇaḥ |
            sarastaḍāgajānāṃ tu viśeṣeṇa śiro laghu ||122||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.123"> adūragocarā yasmāttasmād utsodapānajāḥ | kiñcinmuktvā
            śirodeśamatyarthaṃ guravas tu te ||123|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.124"> adhastād guravo jñeyā matsyāḥ sāgarasambhavāḥ |
            urovicaraṇātteṣāṃ pūrvamaṅgaṃ laghu smṛtam ||124||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.125"> ity ānūpo mahāṣyandī māṃsavarga udīritaḥ ||125|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.126"> tatra
            śuṣkapūtivyādhiviṣasarpahatadigdhaviddhajīrṇakṛśabālānāmasātmyacāriṇāṃ ca
            māṃsānyabhakṣyāṇi,
            yasmādvigatavyāpannāpahatapariṇatālpāsampūrṇavīryatvād doṣakarāṇi bhavanti;
            ebhyo 'nyeṣāmupādeyaṃ māṃsam iti ||126|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.127"> arocakaṃ pratiśyāyaṃ guru śuṣkaṃ prakīrtitam |
            viṣavyādhihataṃ mṛtyuṃ bālaṃ chardiṃ ca kopayet ||127||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.128"> kāsaśvāsakaraṃ vṛddhaṃ tridoṣaṃ vyādhidūṣitam |
            klinnamutkleśajananaṃ kṛśaṃ vātaprakopaṇam ||128|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.129"> striyaścatuṣpātsu, pumāṃso vihaṅgeṣu,
            mahāśarīreṣv alpaśarīrāḥ, alpaśarīreṣu mahāśarīrāḥ, pradhānatamāḥ;
            evam ekajātīyānāṃ mahāśarīrebhyaḥ kṛśaśarīrāḥpradhānatamāḥ ||129|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.130"> sthānādikṛtaṃ māṃsasya gurulāghavam upadekṣyāmaḥ |
            tad yathā- raktādiṣu śukrānteṣu dhātuṣūttarottarā gurutarāḥ, tathā
            sakthiskandhakroḍaśiraḥpādakarakaṭīpṛṣṭhacarmakāleyakayakṛdantrāṇi ||130|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.131"> śiraḥskandhaṃ kaṭī pṛṣṭhaṃ sakthinī cātmapakṣayoḥ |
            guru pūrvaṃ vijānīyāddhātavas tu yathottaram ||131||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.132"> sarvasya prāṇino dehe madhyo gururudāhṛtaḥ | pūrvabhāgo
            guruḥ puṃsāmadhobhāgas tu yoṣitām ||132|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.133"> urogrīvaṃ vihaṅgānāṃ viśeṣeṇa guru smṛtam |
            pakṣotkṣepātsamo dṛṣṭo madhyabhāgas tu pakṣiṇām ||133||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.134"> atīva rūkṣaṃ māṃsaṃ tu vihaṅgānāṃ phalāśinām | bṛṃhaṇaṃ
            māṃsamatyarthaṃ khagānāṃ piśitāśinām ||134|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.135"> matsyāśināṃ pittakaraṃ vātaghnaṃ dhānyacārinām |135|
            jalajānūpajā grāmyā kracyādaikaśaphās tathā ||135|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.136"> prasahā bilavāsāś ca ye ca jaṅghālasañjñitāḥ | pratudā
            viṣkirāś caiva laghavaḥ syuryathottaram | alpābhiṣyandinaścaiva
            yathāpūrvamato 'nyathā ||136|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.137"> prāmāṇādhikās tu svajātāvalpasārā guravaś ca |
            sarvaprāṇināṃ sarvaśarīrebhyaḥ pradhānatamā bhavanti
            yakṛtpradeśavartinastānādadīta; pradhānālābhe madhyamavayaskaṃ
            sadyaskamakliṣṭamupādeyaṃ māṃsam iti ||137|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.138"> bhavati cātra- caraḥ śarīrāvayavāḥ svabhāvo dhātavaḥ
            kriyā | liṅgaṃ pramāṇaṃ saṃskāro mātrā cāsmin parīkṣyate ||138|| iti
            māṃsavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.139"> atha phalavargaḥ | ata ūrdhvaṃ phalānyupadekṣyāmaḥ |
            tad yathā-
            dāḍimāmalakabadarakolakarkandhusauvīrasiñcitikāphalakapitthamātuluṅgāmrāmrātakakaramardapriyālanāraṅga-
            jambīralakucabhavyapārāvatavetraphalaprācīnāmalakatintiḍīkanīpakośāmrāmlīkāprabhṛtīni
            ||139|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.140"> amlāni rasataḥ pāke gurūṇyuṣṇāni vīryataḥ |
            pittalānyanilaghnāni kaphotkleśakarāṇi ca ||140|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.141"> kaṣāyānurasaṃ teṣāṃ dāḍimaṃ nātipittalam | dīpanīyaṃ
            rucikaraṃ hṛdyaṃ varcovibandhanam ||141|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.142"> dvividhaṃ tat tu vijñeyaṃ madhuraṃ cāmlam eva ca |
            tridoṣaghnaṃ tu madhuramamlaṃ vātakaphāpaham ||142|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.143"> amlaṃ samadhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṣāyaṃ kaṭukaṃ saram |
            cakṣuṣyaṃ sarvadoṣaghnaṃ vṛṣyamāmalakīphalam ||143|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.144"> hanti vātaṃ tadamlatvāt pittaṃ mādhuryaśaity ataḥ |
            kaphaṃ rūkṣakaṣāyatvāt phalebhyo 'bhyadhikaṃ ca tat ||144||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.145"> karkandhukolabadaramāmaṃ pittakaphāvaham | pakvaṃ
            pittānilaharaṃ snigdhaṃ samadhuraṃ saram ||145||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.146"> purātanaṃ tṛṭśamanaṃ śramaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ laghu |
            sauvīraṃ badaraṃ snigdhaṃ madhuraṃ vātapittajit ||146|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.147"> kaṣāyaṃ svādu saṅgrāhi śītaṃ siñcitikāphalam | āmaṃ
            kapitthamasvaryaṃ kaphaghnaṃ grāhi vātalam ||147||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.148"> kaphānilaharaṃ pakvaṃ madhurāmlarasaṃ guru |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.149"> laghvamlaṃ dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ mātuluṅgamudāhṛtam | tvak

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.151"> dīpanaṃ laghu saṅgrāhi gulmārśoghnaṃ tu kesaram |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.152"> arucau ca viśeṣeṇa rasastasyopadiśyate |152|
            pittānilakaraṃ bālaṃ pittalaṃ baddhakesaram ||152|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.153"> hṛdyaṃ varṇakaraṃ rucyaṃ raktamāṃsabalapradam |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.154"> pittāvirodhi sampakvamāmraṃ śukravivardhanam | bṛṃhaṇaṃ
            madhuraṃ balyaṃ guru viṣṭabhya jīryati ||154||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.155"> āmrātakaphalaṃ vṛṣyaṃ sasnehaṃ śleṣmavardhanam |155|
            tridoṣaviṣṭambhakaraṃ lakucaṃ śukranāśanam ||155||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.156"> amlaṃ tṛṣāpahaṃ rucyaṃ pittakṛt karamardakam |
            vātapittaharaṃ vṛṣyaṃ priyālaṃ guru śītalam ||156||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.157">hṛdyaṃ svādu kaṣāyāmlaṃ bhavyamāsyaviśodhanam |
            pittaśleṣmaharaṃ grāhi guru viṣṭambhi śītalam ||157||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.158"> pārāvataṃ samadhuraṃ rucyamatyagnivātanut |
            garadoṣaharaṃ nīpaṃ prācīnāmalakaṃ tathā ||158||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.159"> vātāpahaṃ tintiḍīkamāmaṃ pittabalāsakṛt | grāhyuṣṇaṃ
            dīpanaṃ rucyaṃ sampakvaṃ kaphavātanut ||159|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.160">tasmād alpāntaraguṇaṃ kośāmraphalamucyate | amlīkāyāḥ
            phalaṃ pakvaṃ tadvadbhedi tu kevalam ||160|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.161">amlaṃ samadhuraṃ hṛdyaṃ viśadaṃ bhaktarocanam |
            vātaghnaṃ durjaraṃ proktaṃ nāraṅgasya phalaṃ guru ||161||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.162"> tṛṣṇāśūlakaphotkleśacchardiśvāsanivāraṇam |
            vātaśleṣmavibandhaghnaṃ jambīraṃ guru pittakṛt | airāvataṃ dantaśaṭhamamlaṃ
            śoṇitapittakṛt ||162|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.163">
            kṣīravṛkṣaphalajāmbavarājādanatodanaśītaphalatindukabakuladhanvanāśmantakāśvakarṇaphalgu-
            parūṣakagāṅgerukīpuṣkaravartibilvabimbīprabhṛtīni ||163|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.164"> phalāny etāni śītāni kaphapittaharāṇi ca | saṅgrāhakāṇi
            rūkṣāṇi kaṣāyamadhurāṇi ca ||164|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.165"> kṣīravṛkṣaphalaṃ teṣāṃ guru viṣṭambhi śītalam | kaṣāyaṃ
            madhuraṃ sāmlaṃ nātimārutakopanam ||165|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.166">atyarthaṃ vātalaṃ grāhi jāmbavaṃ kaphapittajit |
            snigdhaṃ svādu kaṣāyaṃ ca rājādanaphalaṃ guru ||166|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.167"> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ rūkṣaṃ todanaṃ kaphavātajit | amloṣṇaṃ
            laghu saṅgrāhi snigdhaṃ pittāgnivardhanam ||167|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.168">āmaṃ kaṣāyaṃ saṅgrāhi tindukaṃ vātakopanam | vipāke guru
            sampakvaṃ madhuraṃ kaphapittajit ||168|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.169">madhuraṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ ca snigdhaṃ saṅgrāhi bākulam |
            sthirīkaraṃ ca dantānāṃ viśadaṃ phalamucyate ||169|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.170"> sakaṣāyaṃ himaṃ svādu dhānvanaṃ kaphavātajit |
            tadvadgāṅgerukaṃ vidyādaśmantakaphalāni ca ||170|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.171">viṣṭambhi madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ phalgujaṃ tarpaṇaṃ guru |
            atyamlamīṣanmadhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ laghu ||171|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.172">vātaghnaṃ pittajanamāmaṃ vidyāt paruṣakam | tadeva

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.173">vipāke madhuraṃ śītaṃ raktapittaprasādanam | pauṣkaraṃ
            svādu viṣṭambhi balyaṃ kaphakaraṃ phalam ||173|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.174"> kaphānilaharaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ snigdhaṃ saṅgrāhi dīpanam |
            kaṭutiktakaṣāyoṣṇaṃ bālaṃ bilvamudāhṛtam ||174|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.175"> vidyāttad eva sampakvaṃ madhurānurasaṃ guru | vidāhi
            viṣṭambhakaraṃ doṣakṛt pūtimārutam ||175|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.176">bimbīphalaṃ sāśvakarṇaṃ stanyakṛt kaphapittajit |
            tṛḍdāhajvarapittāsṛkkāsaśvāsakṣayāpaham ||176|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.177"> tālanālikerapanasamocaprabhṛtīni ||177|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.178"> svādupākarasānyāhurvātapittaharāṇi ca | balapradāni
            snigdhāni bṛṃhaṇāni himāni ca ||178|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.179"> phalaṃ svādurasaṃ teṣāṃ tālajaṃ guru pittajit |
            tadbījaṃ svādupākaṃ tu mūtralaṃ vātapittajit ||179|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.180"> nālikeraṃ guru snigdhaṃ pittaghnaṃ svādu śītalam |
            balamāṃsapradaṃ hṛdyaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ bastiśodhanam ||180|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.181">panasaṃ sakaṣāyaṃ tu snigdhaṃ svādurasaṃ guru | maucaṃ
            svādurasaṃ proktaṃ kaṣāyaṃ nātiśītalam | raktapittaharaṃ vṛṣyaṃ rucyaṃ
            śleṣmakaraṃ guru ||181||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.182"> drākṣākāśmaryamadhūkapuṣpakharjūraprabhṛtīni ||182|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.183"> raktapittaharāṇyāhurgurūṇi madhurāṇi ca |183| teṣāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.191">vipāke madhuraṃ cāpi raktapittaprasādanan |191|

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.194"> karīrākṣikapīlūni tṛṇaśūnyaphalāni ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.195"> tiktaṃ pinttakaraṃ teṣāṃ saraṃ kaṭuvipāki ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.220"> sakṣāraṃ madhuraṃ caiva śīrṇavṛntaṃ kaphāpaham |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.221">
            pippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverārdrakahiṅgujīrakakustumburujambīrasumukhasurasārjakabhūstṛṇasugandhaka-
            kāsamardakakālamālakuṭherakakṣavakakharapuṣpaśigrumadhuśigruphaṇijjhakasarṣaparājikākulāhalāvagutthagaṇḍīratilaparṇikā-

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.223"> teṣāṃ gurvī svāduśītā pippalyārdrā kaphāvahā | śuṣkā

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.224"> svādupākyārdramaricaṃ guru śleṣmapraseki ca | kaṭūṣṇaṃ
            laghu tacchuṣkamavṛṣyaṃ kaphavātajit ||224|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.225"> nātyuṣṇaṃ nātiśītaṃ ca vīryato maricaṃ sitam |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.226"> nāgaraṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ vipāke madhuraṃ kaṭu | vṛṣyoṣṇaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.228">laghūṣṇaṃ pācanaṃ hiṅgu dīpanaṃ kaphavātajit | kaṭu

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.240"> kaṭutiktarasā hṛdyā rocanī vahnidīpanī | sarvadoṣaharā

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.241"> mahattadguru viṣṭambhi tīkṣṇamāmaṃ tridoṣakṛt | tadeva

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.242">tridoṣaśamanaṃ śuṣkaṃ viṣadoṣaharaṃ laghu | viṣṭambhi

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.243"> puṣpaṃ ca patraṃ ca phalaṃ tathaiva yathottaraṃ te

            kaphamārutau tu ||243|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.244"> snigdhoṣṇatīkṣṇaḥ kaṭupicchilaś ca guruḥ saraḥ

            rasonaḥ ||244|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.245"> hṛdrogajīrṇajvarakukṣiśūlavibandhagulmārucikāsaśophān |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.246"> nātyuṣṇavīryo 'nilahā kaṭuś ca tīkṣṇo
            gururnātikaphāvahaś ca | balāvahaḥ pittakaro 'tha kiñcit palāṇḍuragniṃ ca
            vivardhayet tu ||246||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.247"> snigdho ruciṣyaḥ sthiradhātukārī balyo 'tha

            kṣīrapalāṇḍuruktaḥ ||247||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.248"> kalāyaśākaṃ pittaghnaṃ kaphaghnaṃ vātalaṃ guru |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.249">
            cuccūyūthikātaruṇījīvantībimbītikānadī(ndī)bhallātakacchagalāntrī-

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.250"> kaṣāyasvādutiktāni raktapittaharāṇi ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.251"> laghuḥ pāke ca jantughnaḥ picchilo vraṇināṃ hitaḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.252">cakṣuṣyā sarvadoṣaghnī jīvantī samudāhṛtā | vṛkṣādanī

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.253">kṣīravṛkṣotpalādīnāṃ kaṣāyāḥ pallavāḥ smṛtāḥ | śītāḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.256"> taṇḍulīyakopodakā'śvabalācillīpālaṅkyāvāstūkaprabhṛtīni

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.257"> sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi sakṣāramadhurāṇi ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.258"> madhuro rasapākābhyāṃ raktapittamadāpahaḥ | teṣāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.259"> svādupākarasā vṛṣyā vātapittamadāpahā | upodakā sarā

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.260"> kaṭurvipāke kṛmihā medhāgnibalavardhanaḥ | sakṣāraḥ
            sarvadoṣaghno vāstūko rocanaḥ saraḥ ||260|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.261"> cillī vāstūkavajjñeyā pālaṅkyā taṇḍulīyavat |

            baddhaviṇmūtramārutam ||261|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.262">
            maṇḍūkaparṇīsaptalāsuniṣaṇṇakasuvarcalāpippalīguḍūcīgojihvā-

            paṭolavārtākakāravellakakaṭukikākebu(mbu)korubūkaparpaṭakakirātatikta-

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.263"> raktapittaharāṇyāhurhṛdyāni sulaghūni ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.264"> kaṣāyā tu hitā pitte svādupākarasā himā | laghvī
            maṇḍūkaparṇī tu tadvadgojihvikā matā ||264||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.265"> avidāhī tridoṣaghnaḥ saṅgrāhī suniṣaṇṇakaḥ | avalgujaḥ
            kaṭuḥ pāke tiktaḥ pittakaphāpahaḥ ||265|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.266"> īṣattiktaṃ tridoṣaghnaṃ śākaṃ kaṭu satīnajam |
            nātyuṣṇaśītaṃ kuṣṭhaghnaṃ kākamācyās tu tadvidham ||266||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.267"> kaṇḍūkuṣṭhakṛmighnāni kaphavātaharāṇi ca | phalāni
            bṛhatīnāṃ tu kaṭutiktalaghūni ca ||267||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.268"> kaphapittaharaṃ vraṇyamuṣṇaṃ tiktamavātalam | paṭolaṃ
            kaṭukaṃ pāke vṛṣyaṃ rocanadīpanam ||268||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.269"> kaphavātaharaṃ tiktaṃ rocanaṃ kaṭukaṃ laghu | vārtākaṃ
            dīpanaṃ proktaṃ jīrṇaṃ sakṣārapittalam | tadvat karkoṭakaṃ vidyāt
            kāravellakam eva ca ||269|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.270"> āṭarūṣakavetrāgraguḍūcīnimbaparpaṭāḥ |
            kirātatiktasahitāstiktāḥ pittakaphāpahāḥ ||270|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.271"> kaphāpahaṃ śākamuktaṃ varuṇaprapunāḍa(ṭa)yoḥ | rūkṣaṃ
            laghu ca śītaṃ ca vātapittaprakopaṇam ||271|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.272"> dīpanaṃ kālaśākaṃ tu garadoṣaharaṃ kaṭu | kausumbhaṃ
            madhuraṃ rūkṣamuṣṇaṃ śleṣmaharaṃ laghu ||272|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.273"> vātalaṃ nālikāśākaṃ pittaghnaṃ madhuraṃ ca tat |
            grahaṇyarśovikāraghnī sāmlā vātakaphe hitā | uṣṇā kaṣāyamadhurā cāṅgerī
            cāgnidīpanī ||273||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.274">
            loṇikājātukatriparṇikāpattūrajīvakasuvarcalāḍuḍurakakutumbakakuṭhiñjarakuntalikākuraṇṭikāprabhṛtayaḥ
            ||274|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.275"> svādupākarasāḥ śītāḥ kaphaghnā nātipittalāḥ |
            lavaṇānurasā rūkṣāḥ sakṣārā vātalāḥ sarāḥ ||275|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.276"> svādutiktā kuntalikā kaṣāyā sakuraṇṭikā |276| saṅgrāhi
            śītalaṃ cāpi laghu doṣāpahaṃ tathā | rājakṣavakaśākaṃ tu śaṭīśākaṃ ca
            tadvidham ||276|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.277"> svādupākarasaṃ śākaṃ durjaraṃ harimanthajam |277|
            bhedanaṃ madhuraṃ rūkṣaṃ kālāyamativātalam ||277|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.278"> sraṃsanaṃ kaṭukaṃ pāke laghu vātakaphāpaham |
            śophaghnamuṣṇavīryaṃ ca patraṃ pūtikarañjajam ||278|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.279"> tāmbūlapatraṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ kaṭu pittaprakopaṇam |
            sugandhi viśadaṃ tiktaṃ svaryaṃ vātakaphāpaham ||279|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.280"> sraṃsanaṃ kaṭukaṃ pāke kaṣāyaṃ vahnidīpanam |
            vaktrakaṇḍūmalakledadaurgandhyādiviśodhanam ||280|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.281"> atha puṣpavargaḥ | kovidāraśaṇaśālmalīpuṣpāṇi madhurāṇi
            madhuravipākāni raktapittaharāṇi ca; vṛṣāgastyayoḥ puṣpāṇi tiktāni
            kaṭuvipākāni kṣayakāsāpahāni ca ||281|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.282"> āgastyaṃ nātiśītoṣṇaṃ naktāndhānāṃ praśasyate ||282|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.283"> karīrakusumāni kaṭuvipākāni vātaharāṇi
            sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ca ||283|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.284"> raktavṛkṣasya nimbasya muṣkakārkāsanasya ca |
            kaphapittaharaṃ puṣpaṃ kuṣṭhaghnaṃ kuṭajasya ca ||284|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.285"> satiktaṃ madhuraṃ śītaṃ padmaṃ pittakaphāpaham |
            madhuraṃ picchilaṃ snigdhaṃ kumudaṃ hlādi śītalam | tasmād alpāntaraguṇe
            vidyāt kuvalayotpale ||285|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.286"> sindhuvāraṃ vijānīyāddhimaṃ pittavināśanam |286|
            mālatīmallike tikte saurabhyāt pittanāśane ||286|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.287"> sugandhi viśadaṃ hṛdyaṃ bākulaṃ pāṭalāni ca |
            śleṣmapittaviṣaghnaṃ tu nāgaṃ tadvac ca kuṅkumam ||287|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.288"> campakaṃ raktapittaghnaṃ śītoṣṇaṃ kaphanāśanam |
            kiṃśukaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ tadvadeva kuraṇṭakam ||288|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.289"> yathāvṛkṣaṃ vijānīyāt puṣpaṃ vṛkṣocitaṃ tathā |289|
            madhuśigrukarīrāṇi kaṭūni śleṣmaharāṇi ca ||289|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.290"> kṣavakakulevaravaṃśakarīraprabhṛtīni kaphakarāṇi
            sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ca ||290|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.291"> kṣavakaṃ kṛmilaṃ teṣu svādupākaṃ sapicchalam | visyandi
            vātalaṃ nātipittaśleṣmakaraṃ ca tat ||291|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.292"> veṇoḥ karīrāḥ kaphalā madhurā rasapākataḥ | vidāhino
            vātakarāḥ sakaṣāyā virūkṣaṇāḥ ||292|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.293"> udbhidāni palālekṣukarīṣaveṇukṣitijāni | tatra
            palālajātaṃ madhuraṃ madhuravipākaṃ rūkṣaṃ doṣapraśamanaṃ ca | ikṣujaṃ
            madhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ kaṭupākaṃ śītalaṃ ca | tadvadevoṣṇaṃ kārīṣaṃ kaṣāyaṃ
            vātakopanaṃ ca, (veṇujātaṃ kaṣāyaṃ vātakopanaṃ ca,) bhūmijaṃ guru
            nātivātalaṃ bhūmitaś cāsyānurasaḥ ||293|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.294"> piṇyākatilakalkasthūṇikāśuṣkaśākāni
            sarvadoṣaprakopaṇāni ||294|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.295"> viṣṭambhinaḥ smṛtāḥ sarve vaṭakā vātakopanāḥ |295|
            siṇḍākī vātalā sārdrā ruciṣyā'naladīpanī ||295|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.296"> viḍbhedi guru rūkṣaṃ ca prāyo viṣṭambhi durjaram |
            sakaṣāyaṃ ca sarvaṃ hi svādu śākamudāhṛtam | puṣpaṃ patraṃ phalaṃ nālaṃ
            kandāś ca guravaḥ kramāt ||296|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.297"> karkaśaṃ parijīrṇaṃ ca kṛmijuṣṭamadeśajam | varjayet
            patraśākaṃ tadyadakālavirohi ca ||297|| iti śākavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.298"> atha kandavargaḥ | kandānāta ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ-
            vidārīkandaśatāvarībisamṛṇālaśṛṅgāṭakakaśerukapiṇḍālukamadhvāluka-
            hastyālukakāṣṭhālukaśaṅkhālukaraktālukendīvarotpalakandaprabhṛtīni ||298|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.299"> raktapittaharāṇyāhuḥ śītāni madhurāṇi ca | gurūṇi
            bahuśukrāṇi stanyavṛddhikarāṇi ca ||299|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.300"> madhuro bṛṃhaṇo vṛṣyaḥ śītaḥ svaryo 'timūtralaḥ |
            vidārīkando balyaś ca pittavātaharaś ca saḥ ||300|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.301"> vātapittaharī vṛṣyā svādutiktā śatāvarī | mahatī caiva
            hṛdyā ca medhāgnibalavardhinī ||301|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.302"> grahaṇyarśovikāraghnī vṛṣyā śītā rasāyanī |
            kaphapittaharāstiktāstasyā evāṅkurāḥ smṛtāḥ ||302|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.303"> avidāhi bisaṃ proktaṃ raktapittaprasādanam | viṣṭambhi
            durjaraṃ rūkṣaṃ virasaṃ mārutāvaham ||303|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.304"> gurū viṣṭambhiśītau ca śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukau | piṇḍālukaṃ
            kaphakaraṃ guru vātaprakopaṇam ||304|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.305"> surendrakandaḥ śleṣmaghno vipāke kaṭu pittakṛt |305|
            veṇoḥ karīrā guravaḥ kaphamārutakopanāḥ ||305|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.306"> sthūlasūraṇamāṇakaprabhṛtayaḥ kandā īṣatkaṣāyāḥ kaṭukā
            rūkṣā viṣṭambhino guravaḥ kaphavātalāḥ pittaharāś ca ||306|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.307"> māna(ṇa)kaṃ svādu śītaṃ ca guru cāpi prakīrtitam |
            sthūlakandas tu nātyuṣṇaḥ sūraṇo gudakīlahā ||307|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.308"> kumudotpalapadmānāṃ kandā mārutakopanāḥ | kaṣāyāḥ
            pittaśamanā vipāke madhurā himāḥ ||308|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.309"> vārāhakandaḥ śleṣmaghnaḥ kaṭuko rasapākataḥ |
            mehakuṣṭhakṛmiharo balyo vṛṣyo rasāyanaḥ ||309|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.310"> tālanārikelakharjūraprabhṛtīnāṃ mastakamajjānaḥ ||310|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.311"> svādupākarasānāhū raktapittaharāṃs tathā |
            śukralānanilaghnāṃś ca kaphavṛddhikarānapi ||311|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.312"> bālaṃ hy anārtavaṃ jīrṇaṃ vyādhitaṃ krimibhakṣitam |
            kandaṃ vivarjayet sarvaṃ yo vā samyaṅna rohati ||312|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.313"> atha lavaṇavargaḥ | atha lavaṇāni-
            saindhavasāmudraviḍasauvarcalaromakaudbhidaprabhṛtīni yathottaramuṣṇāni
            vātaharāṇi kaphapittakarāṇi kaṭupākīni yathāpūrvaṃ snigdhāni svādūni
            sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ceti ||313|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.314"> cakṣuṣyaṃ saindhavaṃ hṛdyaṃ rucyaṃ laghvagnidīpanam |
            snigdhaṃ samadhuraṃ vṛṣyaṃ śītaṃ doṣaghnam uttamam ||314|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.315">sāmudraṃ madhuraṃ pāke nātyuṣṇamavidāhi ca | bhedana
            snigdhamīṣac ca śūlaghnaṃ nātipittalam ||315|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.316"> sakṣāraṃ dīpanaṃ sūkṣmaṃ śūlahṛdroganāśanam | rocanaṃ
            tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ ca viḍaṃ vātānulomanam ||316|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.317"> laghu sauvarcalaṃ pāke vīryoṣṇaṃ viśadaṃ kaṭu |
            gulmaśūlavibandhaghnaṃ hṛdyaṃ surabhi rocanam ||317|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.318">romakaṃ tīkṣṇamatyuṣṇaṃ vyavāyi kaṭupāki ca | vātaghnaṃ
            laghu visyandi sūkṣmaṃ viḍbhedi mūtralam ||318|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.319"> laghu tīkṣṇoṣṇamutkledi sūkṣmaṃ vātānulomanam |
            satiktaṃ kaṭu sakṣāraṃ vidyāllavaṇamaudbhidam ||319|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.320"> kaphavātakrimighnaṃ ca lekhanaṃ pittakopanam | dīpanaṃ
            pācanaṃ bhedi lavaṇaṃ guṭikāhvayam ||320|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.321"> ūṣasūtaṃ vālukailaṃ śailamūlākarodbhavam | lavaṇaṃ
            kaṭukaṃ chedi vihitaṃ kaṭu cocyate ||321|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.323">
            yavakṣārasvarjikākṣāroṣakṣārapākimaṭaṅkaṇakṣāraprabhṛtayaḥ |
            gulmārśograhaṇīdoṣaśarkarāśmarināśanāḥ | kṣārās tu pācanāḥ sarve
            raktapittakarāḥ sarāḥ | jñeyau vahnisamau kṣārau svarjikāyāvaśūkajau |
            śukraśleṣmavibandhārśogulmaplīhavināśanau ||323|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.324"> uṣṇo 'nilaghnaḥ prakledī coṣakṣāro balāpahaḥ | medoghnaḥ
            pākimaḥ kṣāras teṣāṃ bastiviśodhanaḥ ||324|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.325"> virūkṣaṇo 'nilakaraḥ śleṣmaghnaḥ pittadūṣaṇaḥ |
            agnidīptikarastīkṣṇaṣṭaṅkaṇaḥ kṣāra ucyate ||325|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.326"> suvarṇaṃ svādu hṛdyaṃ ca bṛṃhaṇīyaṃ rasāyanam |
            doṣatrayāpahaṃ śītaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ viṣasūdanam ||326|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.327"> rūpyamamlaṃ saraṃ śītaṃ sasnehaṃ pittavātanut | tāmraṃ
            kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ lekhanaṃ śītalaṃ saram ||327|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.328"> satiktaṃ lekhanaṃ kāṃsyaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ kaphavātajit |
            vātakṛcchītalaṃ lohaṃ tṛṣṇāpittakaphāpaham ||328|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.329"> kaṭu krimighnaṃ lavaṇaṃ trapu sīsaṃ ca lekhanam |
            muktāvidrumavajrendravaidūryasphaṭikādayaḥ ||329|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.330"> cakṣuṣyā maṇayaḥ śītā lekhanā viṣasūdanāḥ | pavitrā
            dhāraṇīyāś ca pāpmālakṣmīmalāpahāḥ ||330|| iti lavaṇādivargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.331"> dhānyeṣu māṃseṣu phaleṣu caiva śākeṣu
            cānuktamihāprameyāt | āsvādato bhūtaguṇaiś ca matvā
            tadādiśeddravyamanalpabuddhiḥ ||331|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.332"> ṣaṣṭikā yavagodhūmā lohitā ye ca śālayaḥ |
            mudgāḍhakīmasūrāś ca dhānyeṣu pravarāḥ smṛtāḥ ||332||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.333"> lāvatittirisāraṅgakuraṅgaiṇakapiñjalāḥ |
            mayūravarmikūrmāś ca śreṣṭhā māṃsagaṇeṣv iha ||333|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.334">dāḍimāmalakaṃ drākṣā kharjūraṃ saparūṣakam | rājādanaṃ
            mātuluṅgaṃ phalavarge praśasyate ||334|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.335">satīno vāstukaścuccūcillīmūlakapotikāḥ | maṇḍūkaparṇī
            jīvantī śākavarge praśasyate ||335||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.336"> gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ, saindhavaṃ lavaṇeṣu ca |
            dhātrīdāḍimamamleṣu, pippalī nāgaraṃ kaṭau ||336|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.337">tikte paṭolavārtākaṃ, madhure ghṛtamucyate | kṣaudraṃ,
            pūgaphalaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kaṣāye saparūṣakam ||337|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.338">śarkarekṣuvikāreṣu, pāne madhvāsavau tathā |
            parisaṃvatsaraṃ dhānyaṃ, māṃsaṃ vayasi madhyame ||338||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.339"> aparyuṣitamannaṃ tu saṃskṛtaṃ mātrayā śubham | phalaṃ
            paryāgataṃ, śākamaśuṣkaṃ taruṇaṃ navam ||339|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.340"> atha kṛtānnavargaḥ | ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi
            kṛtānnaguṇavistaram | lājamaṇḍo viśuddhānāṃ pathyaḥ pācanadīpanaḥ ||340|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.341.1"> vātānulomano hṛdyaḥ pippalīnāgarāyutaḥ |341| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.341.2"> svedāgnijananī laghvī dīpanī bastiśodhanī ||341|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.342.1"> kṣuttṛṭśramaglāniharī peyā vātānulomanī |342| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.342.2"> vilepī tarpaṇī hṛdyā grāhiṇī balavardhanī ||342|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.343.1">pathyā syādurasā laghvī dīpanī kṣuttṛṣāpahā |343| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.343.2"> hṛdyā santarpaṇī vṛṣyā bṛṃhaṇī balavardhanī ||343|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.344.1"> śākamāṃsaphalairyuktā vilepyamlā ca durjarā |344| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.344.2"> sikthairvirahito maṇḍaḥ peyā sikthasamanvitā ||344|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.345.1"> vilepī bahusikthā syādyavāgūrviraladravā |345| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.345.2"> viṣṭambhī pāyaso balyo medaḥkaphakaro guruḥ ||345|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.346.1"> kaphapittakarī balyā kṛśarā'nilanāśanī |346|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.346.2"> dhautas tu vimalaḥ śuddho manojñaḥ surabhiḥ samaḥ
            ||346|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.347.1"> svinnaḥ suprasrutastūṣṇo viśadastvodano laghuḥ |347| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.347.2"> adhauto 'prasruto 'svinnaḥ śītaś cāpy odano guruḥ ||347|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.348.1"> laghuḥ sugandhiḥ kaphahā vijñeyo bhṛṣṭataṇḍulaḥ
            |348|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.348.2"> snehairmāṃsaiḥ phalaiḥ kandairvidalāmlaiś ca saṃyutāḥ
            ||348|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.349.1">guravo bṛṃhaṇā balyā ye ca kṣīropasādhitāḥ |349|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.349.2"> susvinno nistuṣo bhṛṣṭa īṣat sūpo laghurhitaḥ ||349|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.350"> svinnaṃ niṣpīḍitaṃ śākaṃ hitaṃ syāt snehasaṃskṛtam |
            asvinnaṃ sneharahitamapīḍitamato 'nyathā ||350|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.351"> māṃsaṃ svabhāvato vṛṣyaṃ snehanaṃ balavardhanam |
            snehagorasadhānyāmlaphalāmlakaṭukaiḥ saha ||351|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.352.1"> siddhaṃ māṃsaṃ hitaṃ balyaṃ rocanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ guru
            |352| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.352.2"> tad eva gorasādānaṃ surabhidravyasaṃskṛtam ||352|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.353.1"> vidyātpittakaphodrekī balamāṃsāgnivardhanam |353| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.353.2"> pariśuṣkaṃ sthiraṃ snigdhaṃ harṣaṇaṃ prīṇanaṃ guru
            ||353|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.354.1"> rocanaṃ balamedhāgnimāṃsaujaḥśukravardhanam |354| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.354.2"> tadevolluptapiṣṭatvād ulluptam iti pācakāḥ ||354|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.355.1"> pariśuṣkaguṇairyuktaṃ vahnau pakvamato laghu |355| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.355.2"> tad eva śūlikāprotamaṅgāraparipācitam ||355|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.356.1">jñeyaṃ gurutaraṃ kiñcit pradigdhaṃ gurupākataḥ |356| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.356.2"> ulluptaṃ bharjitaṃ piṣṭaṃ prataptaṃ kandupācitam
            ||356|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.357"> pariśuṣkaṃ pradigdhaṃ ca śūlyaṃ yaccānyadīdṛśam |
            māṃsaṃ yattailasiddhaṃ tadvīryoṣṇaṃ pittakṛdguru ||357||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.358"> laghvagnidīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ rucyaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādanam |
            anuṣṇavīryaṃ pittaghnaṃ manojñaṃ ghṛtasādhitam ||358|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.359"> prīṇanaḥ prāṇajananaḥ śvāsakāsakṣayāpahaḥ |
            vātapittaśramaharo hṛdyo māṃsarasaḥ smṛtaḥ ||359|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.360"> smṛtyojaḥsvarahīnānāṃ jvarakṣīṇakṣatorasām |
            bhagnaviśliṣṭasandhīnāṃ kṛśānāmalparetasām ||360|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.361.1">| āpyāyanaḥ saṃhananaḥ śukrado balavardhanaḥ |361| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.361.2"> sa dāḍimayuto vṛṣyaḥ saṃskṛto doṣanāśanaḥ ||361|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.362"> prīṇanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ viśeṣānmukhaśoṣiṇām |
            kṣuttṛṣṇāpaharaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ saurāvaḥ svāduśītalaḥ ||362|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.363"> yanmāṃsamuddhṛtarasaṃ na tat puṣṭibalāvaham | viṣṭambhi
            durjaraṃ rūkṣaṃ virasaṃ mārutāvaham ||363|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.364.1"> dīptāgnīnāṃ sadā pathyaḥ khāniṣkas tu paraṃ guruḥ
            |364| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.364.2">māṃsaṃ nirasthi susvinnaṃ punardṛṣadi peṣitam ||364|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.365"> pippalīśuṇṭhimaricaguḍasarpiḥsamanvitam | aikadhyaṃ
            pācayet samyagvesavāra iti smṛtaḥ ||365|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.366.1"> vesavāro guruḥ snigdho balyo vātarujāpahaḥ |366| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.366.2"> kaphaghno dīpano hṛdyaḥ śuddhānāṃ vraṇinām api ||366|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.367.1"> jñeyaḥ pathyatamaś caiva mudgayūṣaḥ kṛtākṛtaḥ |367| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.367.2"> sa tu dāḍimamṛdvīkāyuktaḥ syādrāgaṣāḍavaḥ ||367|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.368.1"> ruciṣyo laghupākaś ca doṣāṇāṃ cāvirodhakṛt |368| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.368.2"> masūramudgagodhūmakulatthalavaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ ||368|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.369.1"> kaphapittāvirodhī syādvātavyādhau ca śasyate |369| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.369.2"> mṛdvīkādāḍimairyuktaḥ sa cāpy ukto 'nilārdite ||369|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.370.1"> rocano dīpano hṛdyo laghupākyupadiśyate |370| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.370.2"> paṭolanimbayūṣau tu kaphamedoviśoṣiṇau ||370|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.371.1"> pittaghnau dīpanau hṛdyau kṛmikuṣṭhajvarāpahau |371| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.371.2"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyaprasekārocakajvarān ||371|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.372"> hanti mūlakayūṣas tu kaphamedogalagrahān |
