          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.375.1"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ yūṣaḥ kaṇṭhyo 'nilāpahaḥ |375|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.375.2"> sarvadhānyakṛtastadvadbṛṃhaṇaḥ prāṇavardhanaḥ ||375|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.376.1"> khaḍakāmbalikau hṛdyau tathā vātakaphe hitau
            |376|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.376.2"> balyaḥ kaphānilau hanti dāḍimāmlo 'gnidīpanaḥ ||376|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.377"> dadhyamlaḥ kaphakṛdbalyaḥ snigdho vātaharo guruḥ |
            takrāmlaḥ pittakṛt prokto viṣaraktapradūṣaṇaḥ ||377|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.378"> khaḍāḥ khaḍayavāgvaś ca ṣā(khā)ḍavāḥ pānakāni ca |
            evamādīni cānyāni kriyante vaidyavākyataḥ ||378|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.379"> asnehalavaṇaṃ sarvamakṛtaṃ kaṭukairvinā | vijñeyaṃ
            lavaṇasnehakaṭukaiḥ saṃyutaṃ kṛtam ||379|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.380"> atha gorasadhānyāmlaphalāmlairamlitaṃ ca yat |
            yathottaraṃ laghu hitaṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ rasam ||380|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.381.1"> dadhimastvamlasiddhas tu yūṣaḥ kāmbalikaḥ smṛtaḥ
            |381|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.381.2"> tilapiṇyākavikṛtiḥ śuṣkaśākaṃ virūḍhakam ||381|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.382.1"> siṇḍākī ca gurūṇi syuḥ kaphapittakarāṇi ca |382| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.382.2"> tadvac ca vaṭakānyāhurvidāhīni gurūṇi ca ||382|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.383"> laghavo bṛṃhaṇā vṛṣyā hṛdyā rocanadīpanāḥ |
            tṛṣṇāmūrcchābhramacchardiśramaghnā rāgaṣāḍavāḥ ||383|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.384.1"> rasālā bṛṃhaṇī balyā snigdhā vṛṣyā ca rocanī
            |384|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.384.2"> snehanaṃ guḍasaṃyuktaṃ hṛdyaṃ dadhyanilāpaham ||384|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.385"> saktavaḥ sarpiṣā'bhyaktāḥ śītavāripariplutāḥ |
            nātidravā nātisāndrā mantha ity upadiśyate ||385|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.386"> manthaḥ sadyobalakaraḥ pipāsāśramanāśanaḥ |
            sāmlasnehaguḍo mūtrakṛcchrodāvartanāśanaḥ ||386||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.387"> śarkarekṣurasadrākṣāyuktaḥ pittavikāranut |
            drākṣāmadhūdakayutaḥ kapharoganibarhaṇaḥ ||387||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.388.1"> vargatrayeṇopahito maladoṣānulomanaḥ |388| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.388.2"> gauḍamamlamanamlaṃ vā pānakaṃ guru mūtralam ||388|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.389"> tad eva khaṇḍamṛdvīkāśarkarāsahitaṃ punaḥ | sāmlaṃ
            satīkṣṇaṃ sahimaṃ pānakaṃ syānniratyayam ||389|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.390">mārdvīkaṃ tu śramaharaṃ mūrcchādāhatṛṣāpaham |
            parūṣakāṇāṃ kolānāṃ hṛdyaṃ viṣṭambhi pānakam ||390||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.391"> dravyasaṃyogasaṃskāraṃ jñātvā mātrāṃ ca sarvataḥ |
            pānakānāṃ yathāyogaṃ gurulāghavam ādiśet ||391|| iti kṛtānnavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.392.1"> atha bhakṣyavargaḥ | vakṣyāmyataḥ paraṃ bhakṣyān
            rasavīryavipākataḥ |392| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.392.2">bhakṣyāḥ kṣīrakṛtā balyā vṛṣyā hṛdyāḥ sugandhinaḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.393.1">adāhinaḥ puṣṭikarā dīpanāḥ pittanāśanāḥ |393| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.394.1">vātapittaharā vṛṣyā guravo raktamāṃsalāḥ |394|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.394.2"> bṛṃhaṇā gauḍikā bhakṣyā guravo 'nilanāśanāḥ ||394|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.397.2"> hṛdyaḥ sugandhirmadhuraḥ snigdhaḥ kaphakaro guruḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.398"> vātāpahastṛptikaro balyo viṣyanda ucyate |398| bṛṃhaṇā
            vātapittaghnā bhakṣyā balyās tu sāmitāḥ ||398|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.399.1">hṛdyāḥ pathyatamās teṣāṃ laghavaḥ phenakādayaḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.399.2"> mudgādivesavārāṇāṃ pūrṇā viṣṭambhino matāḥ ||399|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.400">vesavāraiḥ sapiśitaiḥ sampūrṇā gurubṛṃhaṇāḥ |400|
            pālalāḥ śleṣmajananāḥ, śaṣkulyaḥ kaphapittalāḥ ||400|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.401"> vīryoṣṇāḥ paiṣṭikā bhakṣyāḥ kaphapittaprakopaṇāḥ |
            vidāhino nātibalā guravaś ca viśeṣataḥ ||401|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.402"> vaidalā laghavo bhakṣyāḥ kaṣāyāḥ sṛṣṭamārutāḥ |
            viṣṭambhinaḥ pittasamāḥ śleṣmaghnā bhinnavarcasaḥ ||402|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.403.1"> balyā vṛṣyās tu guravo vijñeyā māṣasādhitāḥ |403| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.405"> hṛdyāḥ sugandhino bhakṣyā laghavo ghṛtapācitāḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.406"> vidāhinastailakṛtā guravaḥ kaṭupākinaḥ | uṣṇā

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.407"> phalamāṃsekṣuvikṛtitilamāṣopasaṃskṛtāḥ | bhakṣyā
            balyāś ca guravo bṛṃhaṇā hṛdayapriyāḥ ||407|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.408"> kapālāṅgārapakvās tu laghavo vātakopanāḥ |
            supakvāstanavaś caiva bhūyiṣṭhaṃ laghavo matāḥ ||408|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.409"> sakilāṭādayo bhakṣyā guravaḥ kaphavardhanāḥ |409|
            kulmāṣā vātalā rūkṣā guravo bhinnavarcasaḥ ||409|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.410"> udāvartaharo vāṭyaḥ kāsapīnasamehanut |410|
            dhānolumbās tu laghavaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇāḥ ||410|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.411"> śaktavo bṛṃhaṇā vṛṣyāstṛṣṇāpittakaphāpahāḥ | pītāḥ
            sadyobalakarā bhedinaḥ pavanāpahāḥ ||411||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.412"> gurvī piṇḍī kharā'tyarthaṃ laghvī saiva viparyayāt |
            śaktūnāmāśu jīryeta mṛdutvād avalehikā ||412|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.413"> lājāśchardyatisāraghnā dīpanāḥ kaphanāśanāḥ | balyāḥ
            kaṣāyamadhurā laghavastṛṇmalāpahāḥ ||413|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.414"> tṛṭchardidāhagharmārtinudastatsaktavo matāḥ |
            raktapittaharāś caiva dāhajvaravināśanāḥ ||414|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.415"> pṛthukā guravaḥ snigdhā bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphavardhanāḥ |
            balyāḥ sakṣīrabhāvāt tu vātaghnā bhinnavarcasaḥ ||415|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.416.1"> sandhānakṛtpiṣṭamāmaṃ taṇḍulaṃ kṛmimehanut |416|</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.416.2"> sudurjaraḥ svāduraso bṛṃhaṇastaṇḍulo navaḥ ||416|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.417.1"> sandhānakṛnmehaharaḥ purāṇastaṇḍulaḥ smṛtaḥ |417| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.417.2"> dravyasaṃyogasaṃskāravikārān samavekṣya ca ||417|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.418"> yathākāraṇamāsādya bhoktṝṇāṃ chandato 'pi vā |
            anekadravyayonitvāc chāstratastān vinirdiśet ||418|| iti bhakṣyavargaḥ |</l>
            <l xml:id="SS.1.46.419"> ataḥ sarvānupānānyupadekṣyāmaḥ | - amlena
            kecidvihatā manuṣyā mādhuryayoge praṇayībhavanti | tathāmlayoge madhureṇa
            tṛptās teṣāṃ yatheṣṭaṃ pravadanti pathyam ||419|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.420"> śītoṣṇatoyāsavamadyayūṣaphalāmladhānyāmlapayor asānām |
            yasyānupānaṃ tu hitaṃ bhavedyattasmai pradeyaṃ tviha mātrayā tat ||420|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.421"> vyādhiṃ ca kālaṃ ca vibhāvya dhīrairdravyāṇi bhojyāni
            ca tāni tāni | sarvānupāneṣu varaṃ vadanti maidhyaṃ yadambhaḥ
            śucibhājanastham ||421||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.422"> lokasya janmaprabhṛti praśastaṃ toyātmakāḥ sarvarasāśca
            dṛṣṭāḥ | saṅkṣepa eṣo 'bhihito 'nupāne... |422| |.. ṣvataḥ paraṃ
            vistarato 'bhidhāsye ||422|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.423"> uṣṇodakānupānaṃ tu snehānāmatha śasyate | ṛte
            bhallātakasnehāt snehāttauvarakāttathā ||423||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.424"> anupānaṃ vadantyeke taile yūṣāmlakāñjikam | śītodakaṃ
            mākṣikasya piṣṭānnasya ca sarvaśaḥ ||424||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.425"> dadhipāyasamadyārtiviṣajuṣṭe tathaiva ca | kecit
            piṣṭamayasyāhuranupānaṃ sukhodakam ||425||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.426"> payo māṃsaraso vā'pi śālimudgādibhojinām |
            yuddhādhvātapasantāpaviṣamadyarujāsu ca ||426||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.427"> māṣāderanupānaṃ tu dhānyāmlaṃ dadhimas tu vā | madyaṃ
            madyocitānāṃ tu sarvamāṃseṣu pūjitam ||427||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.428"> amadyapānāmudakaṃ phalāmlaṃ vā praśasyate | kṣīraṃ
            gharmādhvabhāṣyastrīklāntānāmamṛtopamam ||428|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.429">surā kṛśānāṃ sthūlānāmanupānaṃ madhūdakam | nirāmayānāṃ
            citraṃ tu bhuktamadhye prakīrtitam ||429||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.430"> snigdhoṣṇaṃ mārute pathyaṃ, kaphe rūkṣoṣṇamiṣyate |
            anupānaṃ hitaṃ cāpi pitte madhuraśītalam ||430|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.431">hitaṃ śoṇitapittibhyaḥ kṣīramikṣurasas tathā |
            arkaśeluśirīṣāṇāmāsavās tu viṣārtiṣu ||431|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432"> ataḥ paraṃ tu vargāṇāmanupānaṃ pṛthak pṛthak |
            pravakṣyāmyanupūrveṇa sarveṣām eva me śṛṇu ||432||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.433"> tatra pūrvaśasyajātānāṃ badarāmlaṃ, vaidalānāṃ
            dhānyāmlaṃ, jaṅghālānāṃ dhanvajānāṃ ca pippalyāsavaḥ, viṣkirāṇāṃ
            kolabadarāsavaḥ, pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛkṣāsavaḥ, guhāśayānāṃ
            kharjūranālikerāsavaḥ, prasahānāmaśvagandhāsavaḥ, parṇamṛgāṇāṃ
            kṛṣṇagandhāsavaḥ, bileśayānāṃ phalāsavaḥ , ekaśaphānāṃ triphalāsavaḥ,
            anekaśaphānāṃ khadirāsavaḥ, kūlacarāṇāṃ śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukāsavaḥ, kośavāsināṃ
            pādināṃ ca sa eva, plavānāmikṣurasāsavaḥ, nādeyānāṃ matsyānāṃ mṛṇālāsavaḥ,
            sāmudrāṇāṃ mātuluṅgāsavaḥ, amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ, kaṣāyāṇāṃ
            dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ, madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khaṇḍāsavaḥ, tālaphalādīnāṃ
            dhānyāmlaṃ, kaṭukānāṃ dūrvānalavetrāsavaḥ, pippalyādīnāṃ
            śvadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ, kūṣmāṇḍādīnāṃ dārvīkarīrāsavaḥ, cuccuprabhṛtīnāṃ
            lodhrāsavaḥ, jīvantyādīnāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, kusumbhaśākasya sa eva,
            maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnāṃ mahāpañcamūlāsavaḥ, tālamastakādīnāmamlaphalāsavaḥ,
            saindhavādīnāṃ surāsava āranālaṃ ca, toyaṃ vā sarvatreti ||433|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.434"> bhavanti cātra- sarveṣām anupānānāṃ māhendraṃ
            toyam uttamam |434| sātmyaṃ vā yasya yattoyaṃ tattasmai hitamucyate ||434|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.435"> uṣṇaṃ vāte kaphe toyaṃ pitte rakte ca śītalam |435|
            doṣavadguru vā bhuktamatimātramathāpi vā ||435|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.436"> yathoktenānupānena sukhamannaṃ prajīryati | rocanaṃ
            bṛṃhaṇaṃ vṛṣyaṃ doṣasaṅghātabhedanam ||436|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.437">tarpaṇaṃ mārdavakaraṃ śramaklamaharaṃ sukham | dīpanaṃ
            doṣaśamanaṃ pipāsācchedanaṃ param ||437|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.438.1">balyaṃ varṇakaraṃ samyaganupānaṃ sadocyate |438| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.438.2"> tadādau karśayetpītaṃ sthāpayenmadhyasevitam
            ||438||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.439.1"> paścātpītaṃ bṛṃhayati tasmād vīkṣya prayojayet |439| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.439.2"> sthiratāṃ gatamalkinnamannamadravapāyinām ||439|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.440.1"> bhavatyābādhajananamanupānamataḥ pibet |440| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.440.2"> na pibecchvāsakāsārto roge cāpy ūrdhvajatruge ||440|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.441.1">kṣatoraskaḥ prasekī ca yasya copahataḥ svaraḥ |441| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.441.2"> pītvā'dhvabhāṣyādhyayanageyasvapnānna śīlayet ||441|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.442"> pradūṣyāmāśayaṃ taddhi tasya kaṇṭhorasi sthitam |
            syandāgnisādacchardyādīnāmayāñjanayed bahūn ||442|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.443"> gurulāghavacinteyaṃ svabhāvaṃ nātivartate | tathā
            saṃskāramātrānnakālāṃś cāpy uttarottaram ||443|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.444"> mandakarmānalārogyāḥ sukumārāḥ sukhocitāḥ | jantavo ye
            tu teṣāṃ hi cinteyaṃ parikīrtyate ||444|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.445"> balinaḥ kharabhakṣyā ye ye ca dīptāgnayo narāḥ |
            karmanity āś ca ye teṣāṃ nāvaśyaṃ parikīrtyate ||445|| ity anupānavargaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.446"> athāhāravidhiṃ vatsa! vistareṇākhilaṃ śṛṇu |446|
            āptāsthitamasaṅkīrṇaṃ śuci kāryaṃ mahānasam ||446|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.447"> tatrāptairguṇasampannaṃ bhakṣyamannaṃ susaṃskṛtam |
            śucau deśe susaṅguptaṃ samupasthāpayed bhiṣak ||447|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.448"> viṣaghnairagadaiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ prokṣitaṃ vyajanodakaiḥ |
            siddhairmantrairhataviṣaṃ siddhamannaṃ nivedayet ||448|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.449"> vakṣyāmyataḥ paraṃ kṛtsnāmāhārasyopakalpanām | ghṛtaṃ
            kārṣṇāyase deyaṃ, peyā deyā tu rājate ||449|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.450"> phalāni sarvabhakṣyāṃś ca pradadyādvai daleṣu tu |
            pariśuṣkapradigdhāni sauvarṇeṣu prakalpayet ||450|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.451">pradravāṇi rasāṃścaivaṃ rājateṣūpahārayet | kaṭvarāṇi
            khaḍāṃś caiva sarvāñchaileṣu dāpayet ||451|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.452">dadyāttāmramaye pātre suśītaṃ suśṛtaṃ payaḥ | pānīyaṃ,
            pānakaṃ madyaṃ mṛnmayeṣu pradāpayet ||452|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.453">kācasphaṭikapātreṣu śītaleṣu śubheṣu ca |
            dadyādvaidūryacitreṣu rāgaṣāḍavasaṭṭakān ||453|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.454"> purastādvimale pātre suvistīrṇe manorame | sūdaḥ
            sūpaudanaṃ dadyāt pradehāṃś ca susaṃskṛtān ||454|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.455"> phalāni sarvabhakṣyāṃś ca pariśuṣkāṇi yāni ca | tāni
            dakṣiṇapārśve tu bhuñjānasyopakalpayet ||455|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.456"> pradravāṇi rasāṃś caiva pānīyaṃ pānakaṃ payaḥ | khaḍān
            yūṣāṃś ca peyāṃś ca savye pārśve pradāpayet ||456|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.457">sarvān guḍavikārāṃś ca rāgaṣāḍavasaṭṭakān | purastāt
            sthāpayet prājño dvayor api ca madhyataḥ ||457|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.458"> evaṃ vijñāya matimān bhojanasyopakalpanām | bhoktāraṃ
            vijane ramye niḥsampāte śubhe śucau ||458|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.459"> sugandhapuṣparacite same deśe ca bhojayet |459|
            viśiṣṭamiṣṭasaṃskāraiḥ pathyairiṣṭai rasādibhiḥ ||459|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.460"> manojñaṃ śuci nātyuṣṇaṃ pratyagramaśanaṃ hitam |460|
            pūrvaṃ madhuramaśnīyānmadhye 'mlalavaṇau rasau ||460|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.461"> paś cāccheṣān rasān vaidyo bhojaneṣv avacārayet | ādau
            phalāni bhuñjīta dāḍimādīni buddhimān ||461|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.462"> tataḥ peyāṃstato bhojyān bhakṣyāṃścitrāṃstataḥ param |
            ghanaṃ pūrvaṃ samaśnīyāt, kecid āhur viparyayam ||462|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.463"> ādāvante ca madhye ca bhojanasya tu śasyate |
            niratyayaṃ doṣaharaṃ phaleṣvāmalakaṃ nṛṇām ||463|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.464"> mṛṇālabisaśālūkakandekṣuprabhṛtīni ca | pūrvaṃ yojyāni
            bhiṣajā na tu bhukte kadācana ||464|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.465"> sukhamuccaiḥ samāsīnaḥ samadeho 'nnatatparaḥ | kāle
            sātmyaṃ laghu snigdhamuṣṇaṃ kṣipraṃ dravottaram ||465|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.466"> bubhukṣito 'nnamaśnīyānmātrāvadviditāgamaḥ |466| kāle
            prīṇayate bhuktaṃ sātmyamannaṃ na bādhate ||466||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.467"> laghu śīghraṃ vrajet pākaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ balavahnidam |
            kṣipraṃ bhuktaṃ samaṃ pākaṃ yātyadoṣaṃ dravottaram ||467||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.469"> sukhaṃ jīryati mātrāvaddhātusāmyaṃ karoti ca |468|
            atīvāyatayāmās tu kṣapā yeṣvṛtuṣu smṛtāḥ ||468|| teṣu tatpratyanīkāḍhyaṃ
            bhuñjīta prātareva tu | yeṣu cāpi bhaveyuś ca divasā bhṛśamāyatāḥ ||469|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.470"> teṣu tatkālavihitamaparāhṇe praśasyate | rajanyo
            divasāś caiva yeṣu cāpi samāḥ smṛtāḥ ||470||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.471"> kṛtvā samamahorātraṃ teṣu bhuñjīta bhojanam |471|
            nāprāptātītakālaṃ vā hīnādhikamathāpi vā ||471|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.472">aprāptakālaṃ bhuñjānaḥ śarīre hy alaghau naraḥ | tāṃstān
            vyādhīnavāpnoti maraṇaṃ vā niyacchati ||472|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.473">atītakālaṃ bhuñjāno vāyunopahate 'nale |
            kṛcchrādvipacyate bhuktaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca na kāṅkṣati ||473||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.474"> hīnamātramasantoṣaṃ karoti ca balakṣayam |
            ālasyagauravāṭopasādāṃś ca kurute 'dhikam ||474|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.475"> tasmāt susaṃskṛtaṃ yuktyā doṣairetairvivarjitam |
            yathoktaguṇasampannam upaseveta bhojanam ||475|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.476.1"> vibhajya doṣakālādīn kālayor ubhayor api |476| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.476.2"> acokṣaṃ duṣṭamutsṛṣṭaṃ pāṣāṇatṛṇaloṣṭavat ||476||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.477"> dviṣṭaṃ vyuṣitamasvādu pūti cānnaṃ vivarjayet |
            cirasiddhaṃ sthiraṃ śītamannamuṣṇīkṛtaṃ punaḥ ||477|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.478.1">aśāntam upadagdhaṃ ca tathā svādu na lakṣyate |478| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.478.2"> yadyat svādutaraṃ tattadvidadhyāduttarottaram ||478|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.479"> prakṣālayed adbhir āsyaṃ bhuñjānasya muhurmuhuḥ |
            viśuddhe rasane tasya rocate 'nnamapūrvavat ||479||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.480"> svādunā tasya rasanaṃ prathamenātitarpitam | na tathā
            svādayed anyattasmāt prakṣālyamantarā ||480|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.481"> saumanasyaṃ balaṃ puṣṭimutsāhaṃ harṣaṇaṃ sukham | svādu
            sañjanayatyannamasvādu ca viparyayam ||481|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.482"> bhuktvā'pi yat prārthayate bhūyastat svādu bhojanam
            |482| aśitaścodakaṃ yuktyā bhuñjānaś cāntarā pibet ||482|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.483"> dantāntaragataṃ cānnaṃ śodhanenāharecchanaiḥ |
             kuryād anirhṛtaṃ taddhi mukhasyāniṣṭagandhatām ||483|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.484"> jīrṇe 'nne vardhate vāyur vidagdhe pittam eva tu |
            bhuktamātre kaphaś cāpi,... |484| |.. tasmād bhukteritaṃ kapham ||484|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.485"> dhūmenāpohya hṛdyair vā kaṣāyakaṭutiktakaiḥ |
            pūgakaṅkolakarpūralavaṅgasumanaḥphalaiḥ ||485||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.486"> phalaiḥ kaṭukaṣāyair vā mukhavaiśadyakārakaiḥ |
            tāmbūlapatrasahitaiḥ sugandhair vā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||486|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.487"> bhuktvā rājavadāsīta yāvadannaklamo gataḥ | tataḥ
            pādaśataṃ gatvā vāmapārśvena saṃviśet ||487|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.488"> śabdānrūpānrasān gandhān sparśāṃś ca manasaḥ priyān |
            bhuktavānupaseveta tenānnaṃ sādhu tiṣṭhati ||488|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.489"> śabdarūparasā gandhāḥ sparśāś cāpi jugupsitāḥ |
            aśucyannaṃ tathā bhuktamatihāsyaṃ ca vāmayet ||489|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.490"> śayanaṃ cāsanaṃ vā'pi necchedvā'pi dravottaram |
            nāgnyātapau na plavanaṃ na yānaṃ nāpi vāhanam ||490|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.491"> na caikarasasevāyāṃ prasajyeta kadācana |
            śākāvarānnabhūyiṣṭhamamlaṃ ca na samācaret ||491|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.492"> ekaikaśaḥ samastān vā nādhyaśnīyādrasān sadā |492|
            prāgbhukte tvavivikte 'gnau dvirannaṃ na samācaret ||492|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.493.1"> pūrvabhukte vidagdhe 'nne bhuñjāno hanti pāvakam |493| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.493.2"> mātrāguruṃ pariharedāhāraṃ dravyataś ca yaḥ ||493|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.494"> piṣṭānnaṃ naiva bhuñjīta mātrayā vā bubhukṣitaḥ |
            dviguṇaṃ ca pibettoyaṃ sukhaṃ samyak prajīryati |494| peyalehyādyabhakṣyāṇāṃ
            guru vidyādyathottaram ||494|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.495"> gurūṇāmardhasauhity aṃ laghūnāṃ tṛptiriṣyate |
            dravottaro dravaś cāpi na mātrāgururiṣyate ||495|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.496"> dravāḍhyam api śuṣkaṃ tu samyagevopapadyate |496|
            viśuṣkamannamabhyastaṃ na pākaṃ sādhu gacchati ||496|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.497"> piṇḍīkṛtamasaṅklinnaṃ vidāham upagacchati |497|
            srotasyannavahe pittaṃ paktau vā yasya tiṣṭhati ||497|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.498"> vidāhi bhuktamanyadvā tasyāpyannaṃ vidahyate |498|
            śuṣkaṃ viruddhaṃ viṣṭambhi vahnivyāpadamāvahet ||498|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.499"> āmaṃ vidagdhaṃ viṣṭabdhaṃ kaphapittānilaistribhiḥ |
            ajīrṇaṃ kecidicchanti caturthaṃ rasaśeṣataḥ ||499|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.500"> atyambupānādviṣamāśanādvā sandhāraṇāt
            svapnaviparyayāc ca | kāle 'pi sātmyaṃ laghu cāpi bhuktamannaṃ na pākaṃ
            bhajate narasya ||500|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.501"> īrṣyābhayakrodhaparikṣatena lubdhena
            śugdainyanipīḍitena | pradveṣayuktena ca sevyamānamannaṃ na samyak
            pariṇāmameti ||501|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.502"> mādhuryamannaṃ gatamāmasañjñaṃ vidagdhasañjñaṃ
            gatamamlabhāvam | kiñcidvipakvaṃ, bhṛśatodaśūlaṃ
            viṣṭabdhamānaddhaviruddhavātam ||502|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.503"> udgāraśuddhāvapi bhaktakāṅkṣā na jāyate hṛdgurutā ca
            yasya | rasāvaśeṣeṇa tu saprasekaṃ caturthametat pravadanty ajīrṇam ||503|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.504"> mūrcchā pralāpo vamathuḥ prasekaḥ sadanaṃ bhramaḥ |
            upadravā bhavanty ete maraṇaṃ cāpy ajīrṇataḥ ||504|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.505"> tatrāme laṅghanaṃ kāryaṃ, vidagdhe vamanaṃ hitam |
            viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ pathyaṃ, rasaśeṣe śayīta ca ||505|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.506"> vāmayed āśu taṃ tasmād uṣṇena lavaṇāmbunā | kāryaṃ
            vā'naśanaṃ tāvadyāvanna prakṛtiṃ bhajet ||506|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.507"> laghukāyamataścainaṃ laṅghanaiḥ samupācaret | yāvanna
            prakṛtisthaḥ syāddoṣataḥ prāṇatas tathā ||507||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.508"> hitāhitopasaṃyuktamannaṃ samaśanaṃ smṛtam | bahu
            stokamakāle vā tajjñeyaṃ viṣamāśanam ||508|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.509"> ajīrṇe bhujyate yat tu tadadhyaśanamucyate |
            trayametannihanty āśu bahūnvyādhīnkaroti vā ||509|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.510"> annaṃ vidagdhaṃ hi narasya śīghraṃ śītāmbunā vai
            paripākameti | taddhyasya śaity ena nihanti pittamākledibhāvācca
            nayatyadhastāt ||510|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.511"> vidahyate yasya tu bhuktamātre dahyeta hṛtkoṣṭhagalaṃ
            ca yasya | drākṣābhayāṃ mākṣikasamprayuktāṃ līḍhvā'bhayāṃ vā sa sukhaṃ
            labheta ||511|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.512"> bhaved ajīrṇaṃ prati yasya śaṅkā snigdhasya
            jantorbalino 'nnakāle | prātaḥ saśuṇṭhīmabhayāmaśaṅko bhuñjīta samprāśya
            hitaṃ hitārthī ||512|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.513"> svalpaṃ yadā doṣavibaddhamāmaṃ līnaṃ na
            tejaḥpathamāvṛṇoti | bhavatyajīrṇe 'pi tadā bubhukṣā yā mandabuddhiṃ
            viṣavannihanti ||513|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514"> ata urdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi guṇānāṃ karmavistaram |
            karmabhis tv anumīyante nānādravyāśrayā guṇāḥ ||514|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">hlādanaḥ stambhanaḥ śīto mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit |
            uṣṇastadviparītaḥ syātpācanaś ca viśeṣataḥ ||515|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">snehamārdavakṛt snigdho balavarṇakaras tathā |
            rūkṣastadviparītaḥ syādviśeṣāt stambhanaḥ kharaḥ ||516|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517"> picchilo jīvano balyaḥ sandhānaḥ śleṣmalo guruḥ |
            viśado viparīto 'smāt kledācūṣaṇaropaṇaḥ ||517|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518">dāhapākakarastīkṣṇaḥ srāvaṇo, mṛduranyathā |
            sādopalepabalakṛdgurustarpaṇabṛṃhaṇaḥ ||518|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519"> laghustadviparītaḥ syāl lekhano ropaṇas tathā | daśādyāḥ
            karmataḥ proktās teṣāṃ karmaviśeṣaṇaiḥ ||519|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520"> daśaivānyān pravakṣyāmi dravādīṃstānnibodha me | dravaḥ
            prakledanaḥ, sāndraḥ sthūlaḥ syādbandhakārakaḥ ||520|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521"> ślakṣṇaḥ picchilavajjñeyaḥ karkaśo viśado yathā |
            sukhānubandhī sūkṣmaś ca sugandho rocano mṛduḥ ||521|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.522"> durgandho viparīto 'smāddhṛllāsārucikārakaḥ |
            saro 'nulomanaḥ prokto, mando yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||522|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.523"> vyavāyī cākhilaṃ dehaṃ vyāpya pākāya kalpate | vikāsī
            vikasannevaṃ dhātubandhān vimokṣayet ||523|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.524"> āśukārī tathā''śutvād dhāvatyambhasi tailavat |
            sūkṣmas tu saukṣmyāt sūkṣmeṣu srotaḥsvanusaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||524|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525.1"> guṇā viṃśatirity evaṃ yathāvatparikīrtitāḥ |525| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525.2"> sampravakṣyāmyataścordhvamāhāragatiniścayam ||525|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526"> pañcabhūtātmake dehe hyāhāraḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ | vipakvaḥ
            pañcadhā samyagguṇān svānabhivardhayet ||526|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527"> avidagdhaḥ kaphaṃ, pittaṃ vidagdhaḥ, pavanaṃ punaḥ |
            samyagvipakvo niḥsāra āhāraḥ paribṛṃhayet ||527|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528"> viṇmūtramāhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ |528| sa tu
            vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvān dhātūn pratarpayet ||528|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529"> kaphaḥ pittaṃ malaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syānnakharoma ca |
            netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ ||529|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530"> divā vibuddhe hṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat |
            annamaklinnadhātutvād ajīrṇe 'pi hitaṃ niśi ||530|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531"> hṛdi sammīlite rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ |
            klinnavisrastadhātutvād ajīrṇe na hitaṃ divā ||531|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532"> imaṃ vidhiṃ yo 'numataṃ mahāmunernṛparṣimukhyasya
            paṭheddhi yatnataḥ | sa bhūmipālāya vidhātumauṣadhaṃ mahātmanāṃ cārhati
            sūrisattamaḥ ||532|| </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer"> iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ
            tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā suśrutena viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
            ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||46|| </l>
        </div>
      </div>
    </body>
  </text>
</TEI>
